Current Affairs Commentary

Outlook on the Spanish Turmoil

— Li

The decisive battle between the two major forces of the Spanish People's Front and the Fascist Front, both with international backgrounds, has been ongoing for three months since its outbreak. Currently, the anti-government forces led by Fascist leader General Franco, with the strong support of European Fascist countries, have directly approached the western capital, Madrid. The government forces of the People's Front are actively constructing defensive works in the capital, preparing for a desperate defense. The people in the capital are also constantly marching and demonstrating, with women encouraging men to go to the front lines to fight the anti-government forces for a final victory. The brutal battle for Madrid is imminent.

Following the rapid military advances of the Spanish anti-government forces, more international conspiracies have been discovered. The Spanish National Confederation of Labor has found that the anti-government forces secretly signed agreements with Germany and Italy at the beginning of the rebellion, promising to cede the island of Menorca and the northern part of Morocco to Germany and Italy after the success of the rebellion, and to distribute some spoils to Portugal as a reward for their assistance. Although Germany, Italy, and Portugal established an agreement of non-interference in the Spanish turmoil, they have continuously provided the anti-government forces with manpower and material assistance. Recently, the Berlin talks between Germany and Italy are likely to reach a concrete decision on the issue of recognizing the anti-government forces' government. The French People's Front government is very sympathetic to the Spanish government forces. Léon Blum spent tremendous effort to promote the non-interference agreement in the Spanish turmoil in order to prevent Italy, Germany, and other countries from assisting the anti-government forces. Britain was originally willing to support the anti-government forces to maintain its economic interests, but was greatly alarmed after hearing the news that the anti-government forces had secretly signed agreements with Germany, Italy, and other countries. Because if the matters stipulated in the secret agreement were realized, its hegemony in the Mediterranean would be greatly shaken. Therefore, it echoed France's proposal to promote the non-interference agreement to threaten the anti-government forces. According to a Havas news agency speculation, the anti-government forces seem to have provided satisfactory guarantees to Britain in response to this threat, so Britain is unwilling to make further expressions.

Since Germany, Italy, and Portugal have violated the non-interference agreement, and Britain is hiding behind the shield of the non-interference agreement, standing idly by, it is no wonder that the Soviet Union, which sympathizes with the Spanish People's Front, is protesting, pointing out that the non-interference agreement is a smokescreen for aggressor countries to assist the anti-government forces, and demanding that the Adjustment Committee effectively stop Germany, Italy, Portugal, and other countries from assisting the anti-government forces, otherwise it will consider withdrawing from the agreement and restoring free action. So far, the Soviet Union's protest does not seem to have had a significant effect. On the 22nd, French Foreign Minister Delbos stated in the House of Representatives Foreign Affairs Committee, "If the development of the situation in Spain results in the Soviet Union being drawn into the vortex of war, France does not have any mutual assistance obligations to the Soviet Union. Because according to the provisions of the Franco-Soviet mutual assistance pact, mutual assistance is only obligatory when the territory of one of the contracting parties is attacked. As for the current position of the French government on the Spanish issue, it does not intend to make any changes." From this, it seems that even France, which has common interests with the Soviet Union, is very indifferent to the Soviet Union's protest.

The Adjustment Committee convened a meeting yesterday to discuss concrete guarantees for non-interference in the Spanish turmoil. Judging from past experience, this meeting is unlikely to have any concrete results. At present, the Soviet Union has reached a major juncture where it will either stop Germany, Italy, and other countries from assisting the anti-government forces or withdraw from the agreement and take free action. Germany, Italy, and other countries are bound to continue to adopt a method of outward compliance and inward opposition to perfunctorily deal with Britain and France. The development of this situation is likely to trigger a direct conflict between the two major forces of the left and right internationally.

Confrontation Between Left and Right Groups, Latent European Crisis, Countries Employ Diplomatic Strategies, Clear Distinction Between Pro-German and Pro-Russian Stances

(Berlin) The foreign ministers of Germany and Italy are still discussing today in a dangerous atmosphere where a conflict between fascist countries and leftist countries is about to occur. The foreign ministers of other European countries are also traveling east and west, doing their best in diplomatic strategies. Romanian Prime Minister Tatarescu returned to the capital of Yugoslavia today for diplomatic discussions. It is reported that Yugoslavia has been notified that Romania intends to abandon the French-Russian group and cooperate with Central European countries. At the same time, Romanian King Carol is also preparing to go to the capital of Czechoslovakia to discuss the relationship between the Little Entente countries and Russia and Germany. Czechoslovakia has a military alliance with the Soviet Union, so its politicians may persuade King Carol to improve his relations with Russia. However, judging from the situation in various quarters, Romania seems to have been deeply influenced by Germany. Polish Foreign Minister Colonel Beck has accepted the invitation of Britain today and will go to London for diplomatic talks. Czech Foreign Minister Krofta declared to his parliament today that Czechoslovakia cannot follow the actions of Belgium, because if Czechoslovakia does not ally with other countries, it will not be able to resist any attack. Krofta also denied that Czechoslovakia is willing to be a Soviet air base so that it can attack Central Europe, and also does not want to join the fascist group or the anti-fascist group. At the same time, French Foreign Minister Delbos delivered a speech at the American Club in Paris today, praising the United States' efforts to maintain world peace, and saying that European countries should follow the example of the United States and strive for peace. (National Telegram on the 22nd)

Balkan Little Entente, Chiefs of Staff Meeting, To Be Held in the Capital of Romania

Istanbul, Turkey Military sources recently officially stated that the chiefs of staff of the Balkan Entente countries (i.e., Turkey, Romania, Yugoslavia, Greece) will hold a meeting in the capital of Romania. Turkey will be represented by Chief of Staff General Fevzi. (Havas Telegram on the 22nd)

Polish Foreign Minister, To Visit Britain Next Month, At the Invitation of the British Government

(London) Official sources stated that Polish Foreign Minister Colonel Beck will visit Britain in mid-next month and will be officially received by the British government. Foreign Secretary Eden invited Beck to visit Britain six months ago. Recently, when Eden met with Beck in Monte Carlo, he reiterated his previous invitation, which was accepted by Beck. Political figures believe that Beck's visit is sufficient to prove the close friendship between Britain and Poland, and Poland's attitude towards Germany and Russia can also be explored on this occasion, and further steps can be taken to reduce Poland's reserved attitude towards Russia so that

Results of the Berlin Talks, Italy and Germany Reach a Compromise, Officially Signing Various Documents, Close Political and Economic Cooperation, Italian Foreign Minister Visits Hitler

(Rome) Regarding the talks conducted by Count Ciano in Berlin, the semi-official Roman Popolo di Roma recently reported that the diplomatic authorities of Italy and Germany will sign various documents today to make the understanding reached by both parties official in nature. These documents have long been prepared through diplomatic channels. After Foreign Minister Ciano conducted talks with German Foreign Minister Neurath in Berlin, they have become finalized. Italy and Germany have reached an agreement in accordance with the following foundations: (1) The number of signatories to the future Locarno Treaty and their responsibilities should be limited; (2) Italy and Germany should form a passive joint front on the affairs of the League of Nations; (3) Regarding the Austrian issue, efforts should be made to prevent other countries from alienating Italy and Germany; (4) Italy and Germany should recognize the National Army government in Burgos, Spain, and prevent the establishment of a communist independent republic in the autonomous region of Catalonia, Spain. In addition, it is reported that General Milch, the head of the German Aviation Department, recently visited Italy and reached an agreement with the Italian authorities stipulating that both parties should jointly operate aviation routes in the Far East and open the Addis Ababa aviation route in East Africa, which will be operated by German Zeppelin airships. (Havas Telegram on the 23rd)

(Berlin) Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano held talks with German Foreign Minister Neurath today for an hour. The content was never revealed, and even newspapers did not make a single comment. It is said that the reason for the absolute secrecy of the talks between the two foreign ministers this time is that Ciano could not make any final decisions before going to Berchtesgaden to meet with Hitler. Although the negotiations are currently being conducted in Berlin, the results must be approved by Hitler before the conclusion of an Eastern European Pact and the improvement of the mutual financial and commercial relations between Poland and Russia is not impossible. (Havas, 22nd) Moreover, in the negotiations between Germany and Italy, Germany is striving to avoid causing anxiety in Britain. This is also one of the reasons for the secrecy of the talks. However, according to Italian sources here, the negotiations are satisfactory and both sides are very sincere. (Havas Telegram on the 22nd)

(Berlin) Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano held talks with German Foreign Minister Neurath twice, each lasting only an hour. The relationship is exploratory in nature and cannot be regarded as a final decision. As for what Ciano should discuss with German Aviation Minister General Göring, the newly appointed "Four-Year Plan Dictator," the main focus is on the issue of economic cooperation between Italy and Germany. In addition, Ciano also held talks with German Propaganda Minister Goebbels this afternoon, which must be very important, because Goebbels had a long discussion with Hitler in Berchtesgaden yesterday and only returned here this morning. (Havas Telegram on the 23rd)

Key Points of the Talks Reported in Rome

(Rome) According to well-informed sources, the key points of the talks made by Foreign Minister Ciano during his visit to Berlin with key figures in the German political circles are as follows: (1) Italy and Germany do not intend to conclude a military alliance or military-related articles; (2) Both countries jointly recognize the National Army government in Burgos, Spain; (3) Italy will support Germany's proposal to conclude a Franco-German pact, which will be guaranteed by Britain and Italy; (4) Italy and Germany should support each other in their attitude towards the League of Nations; (5) Germany requires major powers not to interfere in Eastern European affairs and to include the Soviet Union outside the Locarno Treaty, which will be supported by Italy; (6) Italy and Germany should reach an understanding on the distribution of economic forces in the Danube River basin; (7) Germany does not intend to recognize Italy's annexation of Abyssinia for the time being. It is also reported that Ciano will deliver an important speech in Germany this Sunday to attract the attention of international public opinion. (Havas Telegram on the 22nd)

Ciano's Banquet in Germany is Every Day

(Berlin) Italian Foreign Minister Ciano visited the Military Museum under the Linden today, and in the evening, Italian Ambassador to Germany Attolico hosted a banquet at the embassy, inviting all members of the German cabinet, National Socialist Party, and military figures to attend. Tomorrow, Ciano will be accompanied by Aviation Minister Göring to visit the newly built aviation school in Gatow near Berlin. At noon, he will attend a banquet hosted by Minister of Propaganda Goebbels, and in the afternoon, he will go to the "Fascist Club" to be entertained by Italian expatriates, and Ciano will deliver a speech. Tomorrow evening, Ciano will take a train to Berchtesgaden to meet with Hitler and immediately begin talks. On Saturday afternoon, Ciano will go to Salzburg and return to Rome after meeting with press representatives. (Havas Telegram on the 22nd)

Germany, Italy, Portugal Counter-Accuse the Soviet Union, of Violating the Non-Intervention Agreement, Submitting Replies Listing Facts, Adjustment Committee Convened Yesterday, Russian Representative May Withdraw

(London) It has become inevitable that the Soviet Union will abandon the Non-Intervention Agreement and withdraw from the Non-Intervention Committee. The Soviet Union has repeatedly protested that the committee is delaying meetings, so a meeting will be held tomorrow, at which time the Soviet Union will probably withdraw from the neutrality agreement. The Italian Embassy announced today that Italy will respond to the Madrid government's claim that Italy has violated neutrality at the committee meeting tomorrow. Portugal has also notified Sir Plymouth, Chairman of the Committee, that Portugal will also submit a reply within days. Germany sent a note to the Committee listing eight facts about the Soviet Union's violation of neutrality, and claiming that the Madrid government fabricated evidence to falsely accuse Germany of violating the agreement. As for the eight facts about Russia's violation of neutrality alleged by Germany, they are: (1) A Soviet steamer flew a foreign flag and unloaded munitions near Barcelona; (2) On September 12, 60 Soviet machine guns and anti-aircraft guns were shipped to Madrid; (3) In September, 37 Soviet aircraft and 30 aviators arrived in Spain; (4) There were four Soviet bombers at the Madrid Getafe airfield; (5) A British ship recently unloaded Soviet munitions in Alicante; (6) On September 25, a Russian ship arrived in Alicante, claiming to be transporting food, but in fact carried 12 Soviet pilots; (7) On October 4, a Russian ship unloaded munitions and food in Alicante; (8) On October 16, 50 Soviet tanks and 94 drivers were transported to Cartagena. The note also cited broadcasts from Barcelona and Moscow to prove Soviet aid to the Spanish left. (National Telegram on the 22nd)

(London) The Italian government has sent a reply to London regarding the Soviet Union and Spain's accusations that Italy has violated the Non-Intervention Agreement on the Spanish Civil War. The text of the reply is the same as the German government's reply, completely denying the accusations and separately sending an official document to the Non-Intervention Committee, listing the various incidents of the Soviet Union's violation of the agreement to counter-accuse the Soviet Union. (Reuters Telegram on the 23rd)

Lisbon Portugal, in response to the Soviet Union's accusation of violating the Non-Intervention Agreement on the Spanish Civil War, sent a military seaplane to deliver its written reply to London in order to catch the emergency meeting of the Non-Intervention Adjustment Committee this afternoon. It is reported that Portugal's attitude is the same as that of Germany and Italy, rejecting all the Soviet Union's accusations and further accusing the Soviet Union of actively assisting the Spanish government. Furthermore, according to news from Paris, the Soviet delegation may withdraw from the meeting today, and it is said that the Soviet Union is about to withdraw from the Non-Intervention Agreement. (Reuters Telegram on the 23rd)

(London) This morning, French Ambassador to Britain Corbin met with Sir Plymouth, Chairman of the Non-Intervention Agreement Adjustment Committee, at the British Foreign Office to discuss the agenda for the committee's meeting this afternoon and the replies from Germany and Italy to the Soviet Union's accusations of violating the Non-Intervention Agreement. Britain and France are now earnestly trying to prevent the collapse of the committee. If the Soviet Union decides to withdraw, then the collapse is inevitable, because once the Soviet Union withdraws, Germany, Italy, and other countries will be blatantly uninhibited in openly assisting the Spanish rebels. As a result, European countries will be divided into two opposing countries. In addition to receiving the replies from Italy and Germany denying the Soviet Union's accusations and counter-accusing the Soviet Union, the committee will also submit an official document from Britain this afternoon, which is said to clarify that the purpose of the establishment of the committee is to investigate accusations of violating the Non-Intervention Agreement, and should not be divided because someone has made this accusation. (Reuters Telegram on the 23rd)

Philippine President Quezon to Visit China

Manila Philippine Commonwealth President Quezon announced today that he plans to visit the ancient Chinese capital of Beijing on the 28th of this month and will also visit Shanghai and Nanjing along the way. (National Telegram on the 23rd)

Southwest of the Capital, Government Forces Counterattack, Rebel Forces Retreat to the Second Line of Defense, Aircraft Drop Bombs in the Suburbs of the Capital

Madrid Special dispatch from our correspondent with the army on the front line southwest of the capital. After the National Army occupied the town of Navalagamella yesterday, the government forces have now begun a counterattack and have repelled the National Army to the second line of defense. Several aircraft belonging to the government forces have also driven away enemy aircraft. The National Army is deeply afraid that the government forces will continue to counterattack and is now using the defensive works previously built by the government forces to actively consolidate the line of defense. These defensive works are very strong, with trenches crisscrossing, each section having underground bomb shelters, machine gun positions, as dense as beehives, and wire fences intertwined to cover them. It is expected that there will be another fierce battle there. In addition, south of the city of Toledo on the southern side of the capital, the National Army attempted to cut off the railway between Madrid and Ciudad Real, but was valiantly repelled by the government forces. Many militiamen were killed in this battle. (Havas Telegram on the 23rd)

Madrid Today, Madrid experienced its first daytime air raid. Aircraft of the Spanish National Revolutionary Army flew over the western capital twice. The aircraft did not drop bombs in the city, but it was heard that several bombs had fallen in the suburbs. In order to avoid being hit by anti-aircraft guns, the flight was extremely high and quite fast. It is believed that the purpose of this air raid was to scare the residents of the city and make them launch a demand for surrender. (Reuters Telegram on the 23rd)

Talavera According to a communique issued by the rebels, after the National Army continued to gain victories, it is now approaching Madrid. It is heard that the rebels have occupied the Tielmes Pass northwest of the capital. Government forces on the Guadalajara front northeast of the capital are said to be retreating completely. At the same time, the column led by General Franco has besieged the town of Móstoles, 12 miles southwest of the capital. Government forces recently set up a second line of defense there. The rebel artillery bombarded the government forces' positions again today in preparation for an infantry assault. (Reuters Telegram on the 23rd)

Jerez de la Frontera The National Army's radio station here broadcast a message stating that the National Army is continuing to advance in the area of Sigüenza, northeast of the capital, and has occupied the city of Torre Mocha. Although the government forces launched a counterattack once, they were repelled and 250 officers and men were killed. (Havas Telegram on the 23rd)

Barcelona Special dispatch from our correspondent. Government forces in the northern province of Aragon have not yet launched an offensive against the city of Huesca. According to staff officers, the government forces plan to surround the city to avoid unnecessary sacrifices. (Havas Telegram on the 23rd)

Catalonia Province, Decides on a Political Program, Implements a Collective Production System, Unifies Military Orders to Fight the Enemy to the Death

Barcelona Representatives of various trade unions, the Unified Socialist Party, and the Anarchist Federation of Catalonia have signed a common political program, the main points of which are as follows: (1) Capitalist enterprises, except for small industries, will be confiscated without compensation and converted into collective production systems. Subsidies will be given when confiscating enterprises run by foreigners; (2) All real estate in the territory will be nationalized, but small real estate is not included; (3) Military orders will be unified throughout the enemy, so as to continue to fight a desperate battle with the rebels; (4) Militias will be formed to force the people to serve, and war industries will be created; (5) All farmland may be subject to the collective production system, and those who do not wish to adopt this system will be allowed to do so; (6) A vocational group system will be implemented; (7) All banks will be nationalized. (Havas, 22nd)

Rebel Leader, Wins Over Hearts and Minds, Explains Future Political Program, Seeks Welfare for Farmers and Workers

Burgos General Franco, leader of the National Army government, recently gave an interview to our correspondent, explaining the political program of the National Army government, stating, "The National Army government is a government that serves the people and should support the middle class and the poor. It is extremely wrong to say that we want to protect the privileges of capitalism. In the future, the wages of workers in various industries will be proportional to the factory's surplus, and the living standards of workers will also be improved within the scope permitted by the national economy. As for farmland, the National Army government plans to establish a 'family property' system, in which all farmland must be inherited entirely by the most talented descendants, instead of being distributed to all descendants, in order to avoid the fragmentation of land. (Havas Telegram on the 22nd)

British Chargé d'Affaires, Still Stationed in Madrid

(London) Responsible sources recently revealed that the British Chargé d'Affaires in Spain will continue to be stationed in the capital, Madrid. Even if the troops of General Franco, leader of the National Army government, occupy Madrid, the British Chargé d'Affaires will still be stationed there and establish a de facto relationship with the National Army government. Unless the situation in the capital is extremely dangerous, the British Chargé d'Affaires will never leave his post lightly. Personnel at the British Consulate in Barcelona stated that British diplomats will continue to be stationed in the city, but if the Autonomous Region of Catalonia is reorganized into a Catalonian Soviet Republic, it will not be recognized. (Havas, 23rd)

Urgent Meeting of French Radical Party Passes Report on National Defense; Party Leader Urged to Unite to Uphold Democracy

Biarritz, France – At the Radical Socialist Party's national congress in Biarritz, held this morning, retired General Demay (who served as a military advisor to Yuan Shikai's government in China and advocated for the establishment of a gendarmerie) presented a report on national defense. His proposals included: (1) urging the parliament to immediately pass legislation to complete the national organization law for wartime; (2) strictly defending the passage between the Jura Mountains (bordering Switzerland) and the cities of Huningue and Belfort (a shortcut from Germany to France); (3) expediting naval construction; and (4) increasing the proportion of the air force budget. The congress passed this report and a motion praising the Deputy Prime Minister and Minister of National Defense, Dala, for his achievements in safeguarding the republican system and reforming national defense. (Havas, 23rd)

Biarritz, France – The Radical Socialist Party's national congress opened here today. Two aspects were particularly noteworthy: (1) disputes arose between supporters and opponents of the Popular Front, almost leading to disturbances; (2) Dala, the Radical Socialist Party leader and Deputy Prime Minister, solemnly warned party members that France's future would be in danger if the Popular Front were not maintained. After this morning's opening ceremony, the congress continued at 2:30 PM. The delegates sang the Marseillaise, and leftist representatives raised their fists in the Popular Front salute, while right-wing representatives gave the fascist salute, leading to disputes. Dala then urged the delegates to maintain order and delivered a speech, saying, "Our party is a great republican party, and the issues we are discussing concern the fate of the republican system and the future of the nation. We must maintain dignity and a cool head." Dala then recounted the Radical Socialist Party's decision last year to join the Popular Front and its subsequent adherence to its promises, saying, "Our party joined the Popular Front at the behest of its members. This mandate should be confirmed or revoked by us. Also, the achievements of the Popular Front cabinet since taking power are worth supporting, and all of you are asked to decide. However, I firmly believe that you, for the current government's social reforms, although you may not unanimously support them, you must express your approval with an overwhelming majority." Dala also said that the working class has long suffered from unprecedented economic panic, and it is inevitable and excusable for them to cause disturbances in their joy over the victory of the Popular Front. As for the Popular Front, it must still be maintained, otherwise France's economy will suffer greatly. In short, the current focus of discussion is on the economic aspect, which has already transcended the scope of traditional party politics. Therefore, the urgent task is to maintain social tranquility to create an atmosphere conducive to economic recovery. Other party members subsequently delivered speeches, also advocating for the maintenance of the Popular Front and social tranquility, with similar wording. (Havas, 22nd)

However, when a party announces that it will disregard the government's decision and attempt to overthrow the legitimate government with a large-scale movement, the government will clearly tell them that this is not allowed. Belgium cannot accept a government formed from the streets. (Reuters, 23rd)

(London) Imperial Airways' new 17.5-ton airship, the "Canopus," will fly from Cardington, Rochester, to the Mediterranean today. Wang Ying's Bandit Troops Have Long-Term Designs on Shangdu; Wang's Troops Seize Food and Horses in Taolin; Li Shouxin Convenes Seamstresses to Rush Making Camp Tents; A Certain Party Convoys a Large Batch of Munitions to the Bandit Army

Shangdu Correspondence: Wang Ying, commander of the puppet Anti-Communist Autonomous Army, has returned from the Jiabusi Temple meeting. The clamor for a western invasion has been rife, but now, for more than ten days, this claim has become smoke screen. In fact, he has never forgotten the fertile area of Hetao. Amidst this clamor for Wang's bandits to invade the west, figures behind the scenes are actively preparing. Our army is working hard to thicken the defense line, which is within everyone's expectations, and Wang Ying's bandit troops have not relaxed for a moment either. In recent days, a certain part of Wang Ying's bandit troops has been constantly engaging in skirmishes in the area south of Wulanhada in Shangdu County with the cavalry of Zhao Chengshou's unit of the Jin-Sui Defense Army (stationed in Honggertu in the second district of Taolin County). The guard posts of the bandit and our troops are no more than a bullet's distance apart. Although the bandit army often invades, it has never succeeded due to the strong forces and solid positions of our defense army, and has been repelled. Judging from the bandits' purpose, it seems to be testing the strength of the defense army. Later, due to repeated attacks and repeated defeats, they have recently been digging trenches and building ramparts day and night, which seems to be a sign of stubbornly resisting the Jin-Sui army in the east. Wang's bandits also know very well that their own forces are insufficient, so they are making plans for long-term offense and defense. This is also one of the reasons why the war in Sui East has not broken out immediately.

The area occupied by Wang Ying's bandit troops is conveniently located on the main transportation route between Sui, Suiyuan, and Chahar North. Therefore, his subordinates often take the opportunity to cross the border to rob horses and food from the people in Taolin, which belongs to Suiyuan. A few days ago, more than 400 horses were robbed by bandits from the horse herds in Hongqimiao, Taolin County. The Xinghe Security Team arrived in time to recover them. Wang's bandit troops often rob within Shangdu. Such robberies are more frequent at night. Wang Ying tolerates all of them without questioning. Therefore, the residents are extremely resentful.

The Li Shouxin's troops, which support Wang Ying's bandit army in its westward invasion, are now actively collecting food and preparing military uniforms north of Zhangbei City, and are extremely busy. Recently, Li dispatched his subordinates to collect a large number of sewing workers, who are rushing to make several camps for marching and lodging in Zhangbei City day and night. It is said that the weather is getting colder and colder, and there will be ice and snow on the way to the west. Moreover, there are many nomadic people outside the pass, and there are very few houses. Therefore, they are making plans in advance. On the 19th and 20th of this month, a certain party supplied Li Shouxin, Wang Ying and other bandit troops with a large batch of military supplies, which were transported to Zhangbei by heavy-duty vehicles from a certain place. It is estimated that 19 vehicles arrived on the evening of the 19th, including 11 cars of rifles and 8 cars of bullets. 12 heavy-duty vehicles arrived on the 20th, all of which were shells. In addition to retaining some for use in Zhangbei to supply Li Shouxin's bandit troops, the rest will be transported from Zhangbei to Shangdu within a few days to supply Wang's bandits.

Zhejiang Presents Six Aircraft to Celebrate Chiang Kai-shek's Birthday; Naming Ceremony Held in Hangzhou Yesterday Morning; Gong Shaoxiong Reports on the Significance of Presenting Aircraft to Celebrate Birthday; After the Ceremony, the Six Aircraft Flew on a Tour of the Province

Hangzhou Correspondence: The Zhejiang Province Fund-Raising for Purchasing Aircraft to Present to the Government as a Memorial for Celebrating Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's Birthday was organized by party and government organs and all walks of life. Huang Shaohong, Xu Shaodi, Luo Xiatian, Zheng Wenli, Hu Jianzhong, and others were elected as standing committee members, and nine regional branches were organized with each administrative inspectorate as a unit to carry out fund-raising with all their strength. After six and a half months, more than 500,000 yuan was raised, and another 100,000 yuan was raised by the Zhejiang Branch of the China Aviation Association. Six aircraft were purchased together and presented to the government. At 7:30 a.m. on the 23rd, a naming ceremony was held at the Lakeside Public Sports Ground. Huang Shaohong, Chen Qinshi, Xu Shaodi, Luo Xiatian, Hu Jianzhong, Zhou Xiangxian, and the representatives of the nine districts, Wang Xianqiang, Shen Tao, and Li Shanjun, etc., and guests, Wang Jianyang, Cheng Yuanfan, Xu Qingfu, Jiang Jianren, and public officials, students, Boy Scouts, and military police from various organs, groups, and schools in the provincial capital attended. First, Huang Shaohong, chairman, explained the significance of presenting aircraft to celebrate the birthday, and decided that Zhou Xiangxian would report on the preparation process. Chen Qinshi was then publicly elected to perform the naming ceremony and recite the naming speech. It was stipulated that Zhejiang No. 1 would be Hangzhou Special, Zhejiang No. 2 would be Shaoxing Special, Zhejiang No. 3 would be Ningbo Special, Zhejiang No. 4 would be Hangzhou-Jiaxing-Huzhou Special, Zhejiang No. 5 would be Jinhua-Quzhou-Yan-Wenzhou-Taizhou-Chuzhou Special, and Zhejiang No. 6 would be the Zhejiang Branch of the Aviation Association Special. After the naming, the whole audience shouted slogans such as "Long live Chairman Chiang Kai-shek" and "Long live the Three Principles of the People". The aviation school sent a training aircraft to fly low and scatter birthday leaflets. Then, Aircraft No. 1 to No. 6 from Zhejiang were piloted by instructors from the aviation school and performed various technical performances in the sky above the venue. More than 10,000 people watched. The six aircraft then departed from Hangzhou at 8:30 a.m., arrived in Xiaoshan at 8:35 a.m., arrived in Shaoxing at 8:50 a.m., arrived in Cixi at 9:25 a.m., arrived in Zhenhai at 9:40 a.m., arrived in Ningbo at 9:50 a.m., arrived in Fenghua at 10:15 a.m., and flew back to Jianqiao, Hangzhou at 11:00 a.m. At 1:30 p.m., they departed from the aviation school again, arrived in Haining at 1:40 p.m., arrived in Haiyan at 1:55 p.m., arrived in Zhapu at 2:05 p.m., arrived in Pinghu at 2:15 p.m., arrived in Wuxing at 2:50 p.m., arrived in Changxing at 3:05 p.m., and flew back to the aviation school at 4:00 p.m. On the second day (24th), they continued to depart from the aviation school at 8:00 a.m., arrived in Fuyang at 8:15 a.m., arrived in Tonglu at 8:30 a.m., arrived in Jiande at 8:45 a.m., arrived in Jinhua at 9:05 a.m., arrived in Lanxi at 9:15 a.m., arrived in Quzhou at 9:40 a.m., and then returned to Hangzhou.

Nanhui: One Killed and One Injured in Attack

Tao A'er, a resident of Zhoupu Town in the fifth district, has recently been setting up a fortune-telling stall in Tanzhi Bridge Town in the seventh district. Yesterday, after a dispute with his companions over the division of accounts, he returned home. When passing through the Chuanjiazhai area, he was shot and killed. Kunshan: Investigating Corrupt Township Head

Lin Peihua, the township head of Huanhu Township in the eighth district of this county, extorted fishermen under the pretext of collecting registration fees for crab-breaking certificates and embezzled a large amount of public funds from the Bacheng Thirteenth Village Credit Cooperative. After the county government sent personnel to investigate and verify, it ordered his dismissal and strict punishment on the 23rd. The vacancy was ordered by District Chief Lu Jiazhen to select another person to be commissioned.

Thoroughly Prevent Rice Stem Borer Infestation

The county's rice crops suffer huge losses from rice stem borer infestation every year, and last year was the worst. County Magistrate Peng Baichuan has listed rice stem borer control as one of the central tasks of the county's administration in order to thoroughly prevent it, and has used the baojia system to force farmers to jointly control it. The rice stem borer control measures for this winter have also been drafted in preparation for implementation. Starting on the 26th, each district will hold expanded rice stem borer control propaganda.

Changshu: Prolonged Drought Causes Vegetable Prices to Soar

Recently, vegetable prices here have soared. Greens cost 200 cash per catty, and turnips cost about 100 cash per catty. Compared to normal times, this is a sudden increase of three times, causing hardship for the poor. The main reason is the prolonged lack of rain, making it difficult for vegetables to grow. In addition, small insects are swarming and damaging crops, leading to this situation. This area has been suffering from drought for a long time. Since a rain shower on September 15th, there has been no rain for 38 days. As a result, not only is the late rice crop suffering, but it is also affecting the spring harvest next year. Because when the soil cracks, wheat, rapeseed, soybeans, broad beans, etc., cannot be sown. Therefore, farmers are eagerly hoping for rain. Furthermore, other aspects, such as the prevalence of seasonal diseases due to dry weather, are also unfavorable in all areas. Therefore, people urgently hope for early rain.

Wujiang: Careless Fire at Plank Shop and Warehouse

At the Juta Plank Shop warehouse behind the Xie Shang Garden in the north gate of this city, a fire suddenly broke out due to carelessness at 1:00 PM on the 21st. The flames were uncontrollable. After the fire brigades from various sections rushed to the rescue, the fire was finally extinguished. In this incident, all the houses were completely destroyed, burning more than ten coffins, as well as nine large and small coffins deposited by the Zhang family. All were completely burned.

Wuxi: Chen Tiaoyuan Comes to Wuxi to Present Flags

Chen Tiaoyuan, President of the Nanjing Military Council, arrived in Wuxi by special train from Shan County, Zhejiang, on the 22nd and 23rd. It is scheduled for 9:00 AM today (the 24th) at the public sports field outside the West Gate to hold a flag presentation ceremony for the officers of the garrison. The ceremony will be grand and simple. It is reported that Chen may go to Jiangyin for a trip and then take a special train to the Jinpu Railway garrison to present flags.

West Gate Shops Go on Strike

The Yan Yun Ji Fresh Fish Shop on Pengxia Street outside the West Gate of this county was opened with investment from Yan Yunqiao and business was good. At 3:30 PM on the 23rd, Yin A'da, a cook from the Yinglong Bridge Police Station of the 4th Public Security Bureau, bought one yuan worth of crabs from the fish shop, stating that it should be two and a half catties. The employee Qin A'ting tied the crabs with a rope and weighed them with a market scale, warning the cook to use a grain scale, otherwise he would return the crabs. The shop refused. Another employee, Chen A'san, then spoke rudely, leading to a dispute. Later, Xu Dequan, the shop's accountant, stepped in to mediate, but without result. The cook then returned to the station and reported that one yuan of legal tender had been robbed. Upon receiving the report, Police Chief Yang Huaxi led the police to the shop and took the shop's accountant, Ji Dequan, employees Chen A'san and Qin A'ting, and a passerby, Shen A'ting, and others, totaling four people, to the station for temporary detention. The shops in the area, seeing this situation, all felt indignant, believing that the police station was making trouble unreasonably and disrupting the market, which aroused public anger. Around 5:00 PM, all the shops from Xianying Bridge to Yinglong Bridge went on strike, and the situation became serious. The shops decided to jointly petition the Special Commissioner's Office and the County Government to remove Police Chief Yang and the cook, and request relief to pacify the business community.

Planning for Suzhou-Wuxi Road Automobile Service

Since the Suzhou-Wuxi Road was actively opened, it has been fully completed. The road connects Suzhou and Wuxi counties and passes through bustling towns and scenic areas. It is indeed necessary to have an automobile service. Now, Fang Shengru and others, together with Suzhou gentry Li Genyuan and Liu Zhengkang, have launched the Suzhou-Wuxi Road Long-Distance Automobile Company. It has been submitted to the Construction Department for approval and record, and it has been granted exclusive operation rights. It is currently actively surveying the entire route, arranging station locations, and has established a preparatory office at the Qitai Zhan to discuss shareholding matters.

Dried Bamboo Shoots and Melon Seeds Soar in Price

Recently, goods such as gauze, silk cocoons, rice, wheat, and flour in the county have suddenly soared in price, and people's living standards have increased, causing panic. Yesterday, the sundries industry also saw soaring prices for its goods. For example, the opening price of new dried bamboo shoots was 26.5 yuan, and this month it has risen to 36 yuan per dan. The reason is that Jiangxi, Sichuan, Shaanxi, and other provinces are actively purchasing. Melon seeds, such as large seeds, previously sold for 13-14 yuan per dan, but now they have risen to about 21 yuan per dan. Medium seeds previously sold for 10 yuan, and now sell for 17 yuan. These goods are not available on the market because they are being hoarded by various mountain goods merchants. Wuxi has more than 7,000 packages in stock. However, the market price of longan has fallen sharply. High-quality goods previously sold for more than 120 yuan per dan, but now they have fallen by more than 50 yuan, selling for only 74-75 yuan per dan. This is because the harvest in Fujian and the producing areas is good, but the output is not smooth. Hunan lotus seeds, Shanghai Risin brand, previously sold for 48 yuan per dan and now sell for 43-44 yuan, and the market is fair. In addition, the new goods of red dates are looking high at 21 yuan per dan, medium goods at 16-17 yuan, and lower goods at 12-13 yuan. The price is expected to fall based on the current situation, because most people eat old goods. However, each sundries store has very few old goods, black dates are 17-18 yuan, and lower goods are 12-13 yuan, and the market is stable.

Recent Situation in Guangdong and Guangxi (9)

— Our reporter, Xiao An

From Guangzhou to Nanning

After the Guangxi authorities cooperated with the central government, the Guangxi situation is even more of concern to the people of the country. The reporter took advantage of being in Guangdong and made a trip to the Yong River. Historically, the journey from Guangzhou to Yong involves first taking a connecting boat from the southern section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway across the river to Shiwetang. Then, from Shiwetang, take the Guangzhou-Sanshui branch line of the southern section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway to Sanshui River Mouth. From Sanshui River Mouth, transfer to a Hong Kong-Wuzhou transport ship to Wuzhou. This takes at least two days. From Wuzhou to Yong, both land and water routes are available. For the land route, first cross the river from Wuzhou to Rongxu, and then take a car. If you hire a car, you can arrive from morning to evening, taking only one day. For the water route, take a boat up the West River at around 11:00 PM. All the cities and towns along the way must be stopped at, and it takes three days to arrive. Because the river flow is rapid and very winding, and the boats traveling between Yong and Wuzhou are electric boats, it is not easy to travel quickly. The reporter was limited by time, and it was uneconomical to follow the above journey to Yong, so he decided to take a Southwest Aviation Company plane. The company's planes are well managed and have never been heard to have any accidents since they started flying, so their performance has been praised by the people of Guangdong and Guangxi and they deeply believe in the safety of their flights.

Southwest Aviation Company has two routes: the Guanglong Line and the Guangqiongnan Line. The Guanglong Line goes from Guangzhou via Wuzhou, Guixian, and Nanning to Longzhou, and connects with Hanoi in Vietnam. Flights depart from Guangzhou to the west on Mondays, Wednesdays, and Fridays, and from Longzhou to the east on Tuesdays, Thursdays, and Saturdays. Ticket prices are calculated in silver dollars. From Guangzhou to Wuzhou, a one-way ticket is 30 yuan and a round-trip ticket is 55 yuan. To Nanning, a one-way ticket is 85 yuan and a round-trip ticket is 150 yuan. To Longzhou, a one-way ticket is 110 yuan and a round-trip ticket is 190 yuan. Now that the capital of Guangxi Province has moved to Guilin, for the convenience of air transportation between Guangdong and Guangxi, the company has added Guilin and Liuzhou as stations under the principle of developing air routes. In the future, the flight route will go from Guangzhou to Wuzhou, then to Guilin, then from Guilin to Liuzhou, and then from Liuzhou to Nanning and Longzhou. At the same time, the company also plans to open the Nanggui Line, that is, from Nanning to Guiyang. The unification has been achieved, and there is indeed a need to work hard to build the national aviation industry, and it is also because the company's performance is excellent that it has this development. The Guangqiongnan Line goes from Guangzhou via Maoming, Qiongzhou, and Beihai to Nanning. Flights depart from Guangzhou to the west on Tuesdays and Saturdays, and from Nanning to the east on Wednesdays and Sundays. Ticket prices: Guangzhou to Maoming, one-way 40 yuan, round-trip 70 yuan; to Qiongzhou, one-way 60 yuan, round-trip 105 yuan; to Beihai, one-way 80 yuan, round-trip 140 yuan; to Nanning, one-way 100 yuan, round-trip 175 yuan. The round-trip time is valid for one month from the date of issue. The company currently has four planes, all of which have four seats, but because the company is determined to develop air routes, it deeply feels that four planes are not enough. Therefore, it has purchased two more seven-seat planes from the United States. They can arrive in Guangdong in about two months, and it is planned to allocate one to the Guanglong Line and one to the Nanggui Line. It is said that the company has achieved such good results thanks to the planning of Liu Peiquan, the company's managing director. Liu has been engaged in the aviation industry for 20 years and has never slackened. Liu is the most related person in the history of Chinese aviation. Liu has rich experience, so the Southwest Aviation Company he presides over is thriving.

The reporter took the Guanglong Line plane west on Monday. The airport is in Shipai in the east of Guangzhou. The airport is close to the Shanghai-Guangdong line airport of the China Aviation Company. Because the Guangdong situation had not changed long ago, there were troops protecting it. The reporter arrived at the airport before 8:00 AM. Soon, an adjutant from the Fourth Route Army headquarters came to inquire about his hometown, age, occupation, and mission to Nanning. All were recorded in the register. After that, the luggage was checked. It seemed that it was necessary to clarify the origins of those going to Guilin. At 8:15, he boarded the Qiming plane. At that time, an employee of the airline told the reporter that the Beidou plane would also fly to Yong at the same time. Those taking the Beidou were chartering the plane. The Qiming had only one passenger, which was no different from chartering a plane. Let's see who flies faster in the sky. After speaking, they smiled at each other and shook hands to say goodbye. Then, the Qiming took off. The Beidou followed immediately. The time was 8:20. The two planes flew west. When passing over Guangzhou, looking down at the outline of the whole city, it felt very small. Even Yuexiu Mountain in the north of the city did not appear to be very raised. In an instant, it had crossed Shiwetang Foshan, and the villages, fields, wilderness, and trees in the distance were all very beautiful like a garden. However, the color of the paddy fields, some red, some white, and some green, was also a spectacle. Passing Sanshui to Zhaoqing, the various embankments along the West River were very large projects. From Zhaoqing to the southwest, there were gradually more peaks and ridges. Entering the Cangwu territory of Guangxi, the majestic mountains were heavily stacked, and the lush forests and bamboos were dense, forming the appearance of provincial defense. The Qiming passed Wuzhou and did not descend. Because Wuzhou had no passengers and the airport was still flooded, it went straight to Teng County Guiping. Along the way, the towering mountains and ridges continued. The highways mostly passed through the mountainsides, because their horizontal lines were in the mountains and not in the fields. Continuing to the Guixian territory, the fields seen were almost all in the mountains, in terraces, which was quite beautiful. Farmers also built gates to store water between the streams for irrigation of the fields. Looking from above, the reservoirs and streams were as bright as mirrors. This shows that the people of Gui are diligent in production and are unwilling to abandon barren mountains. Passing Guixian and then Yongchun, it is the Yongning County territory. The airline's airport is in the northeast of Yongyuan, so before the plane landed, it was a pity that it could not overlook the face of the entire city. After the Qiming arrived at the airport, the Beidou also arrived. The time was 11:15. The entire journey took less than three hours, which saved a lot of time compared to land and water travel. The reporter then went to Beidou and asked the passengers. According to the answer, it was Mr. Gao from the Guangxi Provincial Bank, because he had more luggage, so he chartered a plane. At that time, the airline came by car, and the reporter took a ride to Jincheng and stayed at the Lequn Club on Gonghe Road.

Changzhou: Discarded Noodles Thrown Away for Testing

The Zhencheng Highway in Jiangsu Province had a private car coming from Jiangyin the other day, throwing noodles along the way in places like West Xiaohu, speeding past. The pie was filled with small fish, fish intestines, and oil. The staff at Xiaohu Station picked up one. The station staff deemed the scattering of the noodle pies quite bizarre, suspecting it was the work of villains, and especially sent the pie to the Wujin Station for transmission to the Public Security First Resident Station. Inspector Zhou Daonan also thought the pie was quite noteworthy, to avoid affecting public security, especially prepared a document to send the pie to the County Public Security Bureau, for convenience of testing to see if it had any toxic substances.

Zhenjiang: Repairing River Embankments Along the Yangtze River

The river embankments of Zhenjiang, Jiangdu, Yizheng, Liuhe, Jurong, Jiangning, Jiangpu, and other seven counties along the Yangtze River in this province are about 200 kilometers long, and are greatly related to the safety of the future of water conservancy in the north and south of the Yangtze River. A month ago, the Jiangnan Water Conservancy Project Office sent staff to various counties for on-site inspection in order to guide the seven counties along the river in flood prevention. According to the situation, it is necessary to actively coordinate the river embankments. It has now been decided to implement the plan. The first step is to start with surveying and organize a river embankment surveying team in the seven counties along the Yangtze River. The principles of repair have been approved. The organization of the surveying team is ready, and Xu Di'e has been appointed as the team leader. Work will begin at the beginning of next month and should be completed in three months. As for the new repair methods and the estimation of construction costs, they can only be determined after the surveying is completed. The strength of the newly repaired embankment will be based entirely on the standards of the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Commission's embankments.

In the Jiujiaba area, three bandits robbed the Yusheng Flower Shop of 15,000 yuan in flower funds being transported to Sanyu Town. In the afternoon, another suspect, Ji Rongfang, was apprehended, along with a portion of the stolen money. Jiashan: Prolonged Drought and Fires Break Out Repeatedly

After entering autumn, the weather is dry and prone to fires. Especially in urban areas where households are densely packed, there is a constant risk of fire. Therefore, citizens such as Tu Huizi propose to petition the county government to ban wooden awnings and reed mats in shops on the streets, and to prohibit the use of tung oil on doors to prevent danger. A few days ago, Wei Zaihe's house in Weijiadai, East Township, suffered a fire and two tiled houses were burned down. Lu Xiaoheshang's house in Fan Jingtang also suffered a fire and two tiled houses and one thatched house were destroyed. At around 1:00 PM on the 21st, Wang Dasan's house, a farmer in the Hongxi Town Dahuo Bang, was burned down due to careless cooking. A tiled house, a large straw shed, and a pig shed were burned down, and twenty-one pigs of all sizes were burned to death. As for furniture and other items, nothing was left.

The Whole City Flies Flags in Celebration Today; This City Holds Presentation Ceremony for Aircraft Dedicated for Birthday Celebration; Ten Aircraft Flew from Hangzhou to Shanghai This Morning; Mayor Wu and His Wife and Others Held the Ceremony Separately; After the Ceremony, Flew to Hangzhou and Will Fly to Beijing on the 31st for Presentation

Shanghai Bishop Hui's Letter to Believers, Praying for President Chiang

On the 29th of this month, it is the 50th birthday of President Chiang of the Executive Yuan. Bishop Hilaire Jasone of the Shanghai Catholic Diocese has specifically designated Sundays around his birthday as days of prayer for China. We hereby publish the notice to priests under his jurisdiction as follows: As we approach the auspicious occasion of President Chiang's fiftieth birthday, this Bishop earnestly requests all priests to instruct their believers to pray to the Lord for the Republic of China and its leaders on the Feast of Christ the King (October 25th) or the Feast of All Saints (November 1st). The prayer format can follow the program of prayers for religious holidays. Indeed, Jesus Christ not only wishes priests to guide believers toward heaven, but also hopes that they instruct believers on how to love and serve the country. He himself showed people the principles of patriotism. Our Catholic Church has always held a respectful view of the country and has never taught believers to sever ties with the country, but teaches them with sacred doctrines and sacraments, so that they are rich in patriotism, enhance the vigorous vitality of the people, and radiate the idea of ​​brotherly love, helping each other, bonding with each other, and making it their duty to serve the country with utmost loyalty and enthusiasm for public welfare. We Catholics deeply know that the Kingdom of Heaven is not in this world, so we oppose the materialism of the communists, but we never despise the rights and interests of the country, disregard the lifeline of the country, but rather, in accordance with God's wisdom, strive to seek the happiness and progress of the country. Therefore, we will pray to God for the leaders of China next Sunday, and especially for Chairman Chiang, so that they can understand where their responsibilities lie and fulfill them well, and that in this critical situation, they can take appropriate measures to obtain the true benefits that the country deserves, that is, internal national economy and people's livelihood, and gradually stabilize, and the international status will increase day by day. The New Life Movement is now popular throughout the country, and we should also ask the Lord to bestow upon the Chinese compatriots to return to Christ, for Christ is our way, truth, and life. And we pray that they will recognize the truth of the Catholic Church and provide all kinds of assistance, so that it can reach its sole purpose as soon as possible, which is to spread the divine kingdom of God. October 21, 1936, Hui, Bishop of the Shanghai Diocese.

The newly appointed Ambassador to the Soviet Union, Chiang Tingfu, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and was busy with various social engagements. Mr. Chiang is scheduled to depart this morning with his wife and Secretary Shi Zhaoying and more than ten others on the Soviet-assisted ship "Northern". The YMCA specially hosted a banquet at the dining room on the ninth floor of the association yesterday (23rd) at noon to bid farewell to the ambassador and invited celebrities such as Cai Yuanpei, Huang Renzhi, Lin Kanghou, Zhang Naiyan, Qian Xinzhi, Chen Heqin, and others, more than 100 people, and Russian Ambassador to China Bogomolov to accompany them. During the banquet, the Secretary-General of the association, Lu Ganchen, gave a welcome speech. Ambassador Chiang gave a speech, which was a great success. The record is as follows:

Lu Ganchen's Speech

Mr. Lu's welcome speech briefly stated that Mr. Chiang is knowledgeable and has a high reputation. Today's appointment as ambassador is indeed expected. This time he takes office to promote friendly relations between the two countries and shoulders a great mission. He respectfully wishes him unlimited progress and thanks all the guests for their presence. With sincere sincerity, please raise a glass of light wine to pray for Ambassador Chiang, a smooth journey, and good health, and deeply hopes that he will work hard to promote friendly relations between the two countries. Then he invited Ambassador Chiang to give a speech.

Ambassador's Speech

Briefly stated: (1) Regarding the relationship between Russia and China, historically, the two countries have always been friendly. Geographically, the borders are connected. Both countries are vast and rich in resources, and their situations are quite similar to ours. Both can be self-sufficient without asking others, and do not harbor aggressive ambitions. They are willing to maintain world peace. In recent years, Russia's construction industry has progressed rapidly, and our country has also made considerable progress in national construction in recent years. I hope to work harder and move forward. (2) International friendship, the interaction between countries is like the interaction between people. For example, some people like to smoke cigars, but I don't. However, I will not refuse to be friends with him because he likes to smoke cigars. Also, some people regard horse riding as a pleasure, but I regard it as ordinary, because I don't like horse riding, but I will not refuse to associate with him because I don't like horse riding. People's friendship is like this, and international relations are also like this. Although the economic and political systems of the two countries are different due to national conditions, the two countries can also be friends with each other, and international friendship will increase day by day. (3) International relations should be based on mutual respect. International relations should be treated equally, without being biased towards this and not being thin to that, so that the relationship between countries can improve day by day and can reach the path of mutual respect, understanding, and mutual understanding. Finally, he said, I am very grateful for your presence and participation, and I am deeply grateful for the enthusiastic hospitality and banquet provided by Secretary-General Lu and the directors of the YMCA. I am really uneasy and express my deepest gratitude. The speech was met with thunderous applause, toasts were exchanged, and the photography was dispersed.

Order from the Ministry of Industry: Register Domestic Goods Factories to Create a List of Domestic Goods for Reference in Purchasing Domestic Goods

The Shanghai Domestic Goods Movement Federation has received Notice No. 1746 of the Ministry of Industry, stating that the Executive Yuan has instructed the Federation to submit a request to the government to reaffirm the government's previous order to purchase domestic goods by government agencies. For cases where foreign goods are still purchased despite the availability of domestic substitutes, reimbursement should not be approved. The Ministry has been ordered to quickly formulate practical measures to ensure rapid implementation. After investigation, the common items used by various agencies, including various stationery, equipment, and other supplies, are numerous in variety. When various agencies purchase them on the market, it is often difficult to distinguish between domestic and foreign goods, or they do not know whether domestic goods are available for these items. This is an important reason for the ineffective promotion of purchasing domestic goods. To promote implementation, a list of domestic goods should be created for common items used by various agencies and distributed to various agencies to facilitate selection and purchase. To ensure complete recording of the products of domestic goods factories nationwide, in addition to the domestic goods items that have been issued with domestic goods certificates, factory registration, and approved for rewards by the Ministry, the Ministry has created a list of domestic goods and submitted it to the Executive Yuan for review, which will be forwarded to the National Government for promulgation and implementation. There are still many domestic goods items that have not been legally registered with the Ministry. The Federation is requested to conduct a thorough investigation and instruct the domestic goods factories to legally register with the Ministry or issue domestic goods certificates so that a list of domestic goods can be created and distributed to various agencies for adoption in succession. This is extremely important, and this is hereby notified.

Jiangxi Province Requests China Communications and Other Four Banks to Handle Agricultural Warehouse Mortgage Loans; Banks Have Agreed and Instructed Jiangxi Branches to Handle

Xinsheng News Agency reported that the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway borrowed 10 million yuan from eight banks, including Bank of China, to build the Nanping section of the railway, including 3.2 million yuan from China, 2 million yuan each from Communications and China Farmers, 1.5 million yuan from Jincheng, 500,000 yuan each from Yumin, Xinhua, and Construction Bank, and 300,000 yuan from the Postal Savings Bureau. From February to October this year, 6.1 million yuan has been disbursed. Now, due to the order to complete the opening of the railway by the end of March next year, earthwork, bridge, and culvert projects are being built day and night, and there is an urgent need for funds. Therefore, Zhang Zili, the Secretary-General of the Joint Company of the railway, arrived in Shanghai from Hangzhou to discuss with the syndicate of banks to change the disbursement method. The Nanping Railway Loan Syndicate held a temporary meeting at the Bank of China on the Bund yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. Huo Baoshu from China, Cao Jiru from Communications, Xiong Baosun from China Farmers, Qian Chengxin from Jiangxi Yumin, Wang Zhixin from Xinhua, and Wu Yunzhai from Jincheng attended. Zhang Zili, the Secretary-General of the Railway Council, attended as an observer. Huo Baoshu, the chairman, first reported the purpose of the meeting, followed by Zhang Zili, who stated the process of completing the project early according to the order. It was decided on the spot that the disbursement would be increased by 200,000 yuan per month from November, totaling 700,000 yuan, to be cleared by the end of April next year. The meeting adjourned at about 5:00 PM. Secretary Zhang is scheduled to return to Hangzhou this morning.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's River Vessels Successfully Reformed, Equipment Clean and Passengers Comfortable

Since the reform of the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the repair of ships, the addition of equipment, and the improvement of cabins have all been aimed at passenger safety and comfort. By the end of June this year, the statistics of passenger income increased by more than 438,000 yuan compared with the previous year. Now, Chen Xiaozeng, the director of the Ship Department, in order to seek further improvement, will thoroughly reform the equipment of the Yangtze River ships again. The ones that have been successfully implemented are: (1) The toilet in the special-class room has insufficient flushing pressure and is not easy to clean due to the small capacity of the water tank and the improper layout of the pipes. It has been completely renovated. The toilets and bathrooms in the first-class cabin are not enough for use. Now it has been decided to convert one of the two open rooms in each ship into male and female bathrooms. The remaining space in the middle corridor will be used as a luggage storage room and fitted with folding doors. The original toilet is enlarged and used exclusively for female passengers, and the bathroom and toilet outside the right side are completely converted into male toilets. A vacant lot will be carved out behind the living room and new rooms will be added to make up for the original shortage. In the second-floor cabin, two second-class rooms have been vacated for three feet each in the offices of the purser and the tally clerk to install four conveniences for use by male and female passengers. The original lamp room has been converted into a beverage and washing room. The rear end of the third-floor cabin has been converted into a toilet, combined with the original one, which can be used separately by men and women. (2) The third-class cabin service personnel used to have no fixed berths and lived in various places. Now, 20 new three-tiered beds have been installed at the rear end, with stepping boards added to the sides of the beds and 12 new wooden cabinets with 48 drawers. Each service personnel is in charge of one to store passengers' other items. A layer of seven-foot-high square-eyed wire mesh is newly installed along the right end to be careful. The tarpaulin that encloses the wind and rain also has transparent soft film windows to make the light bright. The kitchen utensils and chopping tables used to be placed in the pedestrian aisle, which obstructed traffic and cleanliness. Now, a large room in front of the kitchen (where the kitchen servants' other items used to be stacked) has been converted into kitchen utensils, and an iron shed has been installed in the south passageway to place and hang vegetables. The sailors' kitchen originally had a separate room, but now all the food is supplied by the main kitchen. This room has been used as a hot water supply room for the entire ship. The third-class cabin originally had no luggage room. Now, part of the crew's storage room on the upper floor has been carved out to store third-class passengers' luggage, but it does not hinder the opening and closing of the water tank at the stern. The third-class passengers' beds were originally two-tiered beds. Passengers on the upper tier would borrow tea servants' boxes and cabinets as stepping feet up and down. Now, all the boxes and cabinets have been removed and stepping boards have been installed between the two beds to facilitate passengers getting on and off. In addition, third-class passengers used to eat on the counter. Now, orange tables have been added in a considerable open space so that third-class passengers can dine together very comfortably. A new water tank with a filtering machine has been installed on the upper platform for the use of first, second, and third-class passengers. The water tanks that were scattered everywhere before have been removed. After this thorough improvement of the Yangtze River ships of the bureau, it is not only the happiness of the passengers up and down the water, but also no different from the extremely neat and standardized postal ships in the Yangtze River. The foreign merchant ships, which were known for their cleanliness, have been eclipsed by them from now on.

Investigation of Foreign Banks in China, Total of 30, Jardine Matheson Is the Oldest, HSBC and Yokohama Specie Bank Have the Most Branches

Up to this year, there are a total of 30 foreign banks that have established headquarters and branches in our country. (7) There is one Italian bank, namely, Huayi. (8) There is one German bank, namely, Dehua. (9) There is one Russian bank, namely, Moscow National. (10) There is one French-Belgian joint venture bank, namely, Yipin Fangkuan. (11) There is one Sino-French joint venture bank, namely, Sino-French Industrial and Commercial. The British HSBC and the Japanese Yokohama Specie Bank have the most branches in China, with 12 each. The above banks all operate foreign exchange business.

Resignation: German Consul-General Departs Shanghai

A dispatch from the National Maritime News Agency in Shanghai, dated October 23rd, states that Dr. Betz, the former German Consul-General in Tianjin, has resigned and is preparing to return to his home country. He made a brief stop in Shanghai before heading to Southern China, where he will board a German ship from Hong Kong to return home. Dr. Betz first came to China in 1898, serving at the German Consulate-General in Shanghai. After residing in China for some time, he participated in the German Marine Corps' relief of Tianjin during the Boxer Rebellion in 1900. The following year, he was reassigned to the German Consulate in Niuzhuang, and later served in Shantou and Jinan. Betz also traveled extensively in the Sichuan interior. From 1907 to 1908, he served as a translator at the German Embassy in Beijing. In 1909, he was appointed Consul-General in Tianjin. In 1917, Betz returned to Germany to serve in the war effort, earning the rank of captain. From 1920 to 192- [sic, likely 1930] Dr. Betz served in the Berlin Foreign Office. In 1931, he was reappointed Consul-General in Tianjin. Since 1929, Dr. Betz had been elected leader of the Tianjin diplomatic corps.

Interview with Consul-General to Sydney, Bao Junjian: Departing Next Month for His Post, Earnestly Seeking Guidance from All Quarters

The newly appointed Consul-General to Sydney, Australia, Bao Junjian, is a native of Nantong, Jiangsu Province, and a renowned domestic economist. He is also rich in experience in administrative and diplomatic affairs. After returning from studying in the United States, he has served in both the North and South for more than a decade, with excellent results. Most recently, he served as a member of the Treaty Committee in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, where he was known for his diligence. He succeeds Mr. Chen Weiping, the former Consul-General in Sydney, who resigned for personal reasons. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs immediately appointed Mr. Bao as his replacement. According to Bao, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has recently been actively adjusting the responsibilities of overseas embassies and consulates, striving for improvements. As a consular official, he is aware of his own limited knowledge and abilities. After taking office, he will follow the orders of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, serving with loyalty, diligence, and prudence. Any suggestions or areas that he believes need improvement will be reported in advance for approval before being implemented. Therefore, he has no specific opinions on the work, only a desire to carefully study how to work hard. Regarding matters such as protecting overseas Chinese, promoting domestic goods, and promoting trade, many public and private organizations both domestically and abroad are studying these issues. There are also many Party and national leaders, people familiar with the situation in Australia, and returned overseas Chinese who are serving in various sectors. He intends to visit them separately to seek their guidance. He has heard that although overseas Chinese in Australia have been affected by the global economic downturn in recent years, they have been able to maintain their livelihoods due to their diligence and hard work. Furthermore, Sino-Australian trade has recently shown signs of improvement. If all parties can promote it and work together, it will not be difficult to achieve our goals. Recently, the staff of our country's Party headquarters in Australia are all loyal comrades who have made great achievements in promoting Party affairs and promoting overseas Chinese education. After taking office, he believes that he will be able to obtain their guidance, follow the principles of the Party and the nation, and do something together for the overseas Chinese. As for the date of his departure, given the heavy workload of the Sydney consulate, he has been actively preparing to leave for his post in late next month, traveling from Shanghai to Hong Kong and then directly to his post in Australia.

National Unified Sales System for the Coal Mining Industry: Expected to be Implemented Next Spring

After the establishment of the general office of the National Coal Mining Industry Joint Office in Wuhan, and the Shanghai branches, the Hankou and Beiping-Tianjin branches have also been organized, with the Qingdao-Jinan branch still in preparation. Unified sales are expected to be implemented from January next year. The details are as follows:

Wuhan Branch

The Wuhan Branch is located in Hankou and its area covers the three towns of Wuhan, the ports along the Yangtze River from Jiujiang upwards, the northern section of the Yuehan Railway, and the southern section of the Pinghan Railway. The member companies include Zhongfu, Yili, Liuhegou, and seven others. During the inaugural meeting, Xu Weirong, Li Zucai, and Li Zufeng were mutually elected as standing committee members, and the articles of association were passed and submitted to the general office for referral to the Ministry for registration.

Beiping-Tianjin Branch

The Beiping-Tianjin Branch is located in Beiping and its area covers the cities of Beiping and Tianjin, the stations along the Beijing-Shenyang Railway, the northern section of the Pinghan Railway, and the PingSui Railway. The member companies include Kai Ao, Jinbei, Baojin, Jingxing, Datong, Mentougou, Zhengfeng, Yu Bao, Yili, Liuhegou, and ten others. At the inaugural meeting, the articles of association were passed and it was decided to elect five standing committee members, with the mining companies serving as committee members. Kai Ao, Jingxing, Datong, Mentougou, and Xing Bao were appointed. The Qingdao-Jinan branch is still in preparation.

Beijing-Shanghai Budget

According to Article 10 of the General Office's Articles of Association, members of each branch should submit their production and sales budgets for the six months from July and January of the following year during April and October each year, stipulating the allocation of sales volume for each mine, etc. Currently, the mines in the Beijing-Shanghai branch have submitted their budgets, and the office is investigating each mine separately, striving to negotiate the sales volume and price by the end of the year so that it can be implemented from January next year. The other branches, such as Beiping-Tianjin and Wuhan, are also proceeding separately.

Xinli Woolen Mill: Criminal Lawsuit Filed Between Shareholders; Huang Pinliang Sues Lin Mengfei, et al.; Defendants Claim Goods Were Used to Offset Debt

Huang Pinliang (Huang Ruiming), a Ningbo native who is a shareholder and manager of the currently closed Xinli Woolen Mill, hired lawyer Yuan Yang'an to file a self-accusation in the First Special District District Court against Lin Mengfei, a shareholder of the mill and former vice president of the Ningbo Chamber of Commerce, and Sun Baowen, a shareholder and deputy manager of the mill, and Sun Baoshou, the accountant, for embezzlement and breach of trust. The court has summoned them for trial. Because the defendants have not surrendered, the order was postponed, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng opened the court and summoned both parties for questioning. According to Huang Pinliang, he and Baowen each recognized four shares, each share worth 1,000 taels of silver, and Lin recognized one share. Lin served as the supervisor, he served as the manager, and Baowen served as the deputy manager, and Baoshou was hired as the accountant. At the end of last year, he suffered from eye disease and could not go to the factory to handle matters. The defendants secretly moved and hid the goods and raw materials stored in the factory, worth more than 5,600 yuan, in the shop set up by Lin in the Rising Sun Lane on the Great Road, causing Xinli to be unable to operate and to shut down on January 18. In addition, when checking the account deposits, as of January 25, there should have been more than 760 yuan in deposits, but Baoshou only wrote that there were more than 160 yuan, a shortage of 600 yuan, and even this more than 160 yuan has disappeared. When questioned, Lin Mengfei stated that he was the manager of the Taihan Qianzhuang in Ningbo, and Xinli owed the Qianzhuang 8,000 yuan. After the Qianzhuang was liquidated last autumn, they repeatedly demanded payment but were ignored. Therefore, at the end of the year, he came to Shanghai to demand payment in person. The factory had no cash, so it used the stored goods as collateral. After selling the goods and paying off the debt, there was still more than 4,700 yuan owed. Lawyer Yuan Hanyun was hired to present the Taihan's lawsuit filed in the Civil Court this autumn against Xinli for failing to repay the debt, proving that the plaintiff's accusation of embezzlement and breach of trust actually contained a confrontational effect. According to Sun Baowen, using the goods as collateral for the debt owed to Taihan was ordered by the plaintiff to him and Lin to negotiate, and when the goods were transported to Lin's shop, the plaintiff was also present at the factory. Furthermore, the receipt issued by Lin for receiving the goods was given to the plaintiff for safekeeping, so how could he pretend not to know? Sun Baoshou stated that he returned to Ningbo on January 17 due to business matters. All the money in the account was handed over to the plaintiff, so the account from January 17 to January 25 should have been managed by someone appointed by the plaintiff. If there were any errors, he would not be responsible and it could be easily clarified by checking the handwriting. Lawyers He Xianzhang and others were also hired to defend. The court then ordered that the trial be postponed. The defendants Sun Shiwen and Sun Baoshou were released on bail by their defense lawyers He Xianzhang and Feng Meixue, and they were ordered to appear at any time.
