The Jiangwan Teng Peifu Kindergarten was founded by Ms. Guo Baoyi and is managed by Ms. Sang Wenlan. The management is effective and the results are excellent. For two years, the financial aspects have also been maintained. However, due to the situation, the kindergarten has temporarily suspended classes. According to founder Guo Baoyi, due to the tense situation and the unsafe location, all the students are very young, and she is afraid that the protection aspect may not be complete. Therefore, she announced the temporary suspension of classes two weeks ago. It is currently difficult to say how the situation will develop, but if there is a guarantee of safety, the kindergarten will notify all parents and schedule the resumption of classes. It is also understood that Ms. Guo now has a temporary office at Room 436, No. 131 Museum Road.

Renji Hospital Report: Medical Affairs for September and the Feng Family's Donation

Renji Hospital's report for September of this year: 15,717 outpatient visits, 362 new inpatients, 6,553 inpatient days, an average of 460 people provided with meals each month, 43 male suicides, 46 female suicides, 421 emergency surgical cases, 48 emergency surgical cases due to factory accidents, 425 patients sent by the Public Concession police, 57 patients sent by the French Concession police, and 28 deliveries. Judging from the above statistics for September, the work in September was not much different from the work in the previous month. Suicides have decreased significantly, but emergency surgical cases due to factory accidents have increased sharply, with the most painful being acid burns, which may disfigure the patient for life. There are many cases of dysentery in the outpatient department, and malignant malaria is also quite prevalent. The records in the obstetrics department have increased even more. In the first half of the month, all the hospital wards were full, which is the first time in the hospital's history. There have been slight changes in senior staff. Dr. Wang Baozhen has left his position, which has been replaced by Dr. Huang Huiguang. This month, there is a novel event that is worth mentioning, which shows that the hospital's friends have deep sympathy and practical attention to the hospital's work. That is, Mr. Feng Bingnan allocated the gift money received when his son Zhensheng married Ms. Zhang Bingjun as a special donation. Mr. Feng anticipated that his relatives and friends would give valuable gifts, so he notified his relatives and friends in advance to give cash gifts, each not exceeding ten yuan, and divided the gift money equally between Renji and Sacred Heart Hospitals. The total amount received by this hospital was about 3,500 yuan. The hospital expresses its sincere gratitude to Mr. Feng for his kind act and to the newlyweds, and wishes the newlyweds happiness in the future, and hopes that other friends of the hospital will follow Mr. Feng's example to support the hospital.

Domestic Towel Industry Announces Price Increase of 20%

Recently, the prices of yarn and cotton raw materials in the market have soared. The yarn and cotton industries have been holding meetings to discuss price increases to ensure their capital. Yesterday, the Shanghai National Towel Industry Association also issued a notice to its customers regarding the increase in the price of its products: "Due to the soaring price of Yilai cotton yarn, the cost of production for the industry has increased sharply, and it is necessary to seek relief quickly. Therefore, an emergency meeting of all industry members was convened, and it was decided that from today, the prices of various towels and cotton textiles will be increased by 20% based on the recent selling prices in order to maintain capital. If the price of yarn continues to rise, another meeting will be convened to discuss further increases. We hope that all customers will understand."

Details of the Murder of Japanese Sailor Tagako in Tianjing: The Zhang Ronghe Case Concludes - Zhang Testifies He Did Not Conceal Evidence for Someone Else - Police Lawyer and Defense Counsel Argue

Zhang Ronghe, a Tai Zhou porridge vendor, because he hid a box cannon, the murder weapon used in the shooting of Japanese sailor Asao Tagako in the Wu Song Road, Hai Ning Road incident of the 23rd of last month, inside a sand box in No. 15 Alley of Hai Ning Road, was arrested. The Hong Kou police department then prosecuted him in the First Special District Court for the crime of destroying evidence under Article 165 of the Criminal Code. The court, under Judge Zhong Qing, repeatedly held court sessions to investigate the situation, as already reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhong continued the hearing in the criminal division. Zhang Ronghe's father, Zhang Wenshan (age 60), and lawyers Yu Hua and Jin Zhi came to court to defend him, while Prosecutor Tang Peiyou also attended to perform his duties. First, the police lawyer, Zhang Shizhu, stated that during the adjournment, there had been no new developments in the case. The court then questioned Zhang Ronghe. According to Zhang, after hearing the gunshot, he suspected that his fellow villager, Zhang Tai, had been shot, so he rushed to investigate. On his way to the scene, he kicked a pistol, picked it up, and hid it in the sand box, intending to report it to the police later. The court questioned him whether he intended to sell the gun, seek a reward, or conceal evidence for the perpetrator after hiding the gun. He replied that he intended to report the matter to the police, and whether he would receive a reward was up to the police department, and he did not conceal evidence for someone else. Judge Zhong, believing that the facts of the case were clear, ordered the commencement of the debate. The police lawyer Zhang then argued that the gun seized in this case had been proven to be the weapon used to shoot Tagako and others, and the defendant had confessed to hiding the pistol both to the police and in court, and it had been confirmed by witnesses such as Japanese national Horie Tadashi. Therefore, there was no doubt about the defendant's criminal behavior, and his awareness that the gun was a murder weapon and his act of concealing it clearly demonstrated his criminal intent. As for the reason for his crime, whether it was to seek a reward or to sell the gun, it did not affect the establishment of the crime itself and should only be used by the court as a reference when sentencing. He requested that the court sentence him according to Article 165 of the Criminal Code. Judge Zhong then asked Zhang Ronghe how long it took him to reach the scene after hearing the gunshot. He replied that it took him about half a cigarette's time. The lawyer then defended Zhang, stating that according to Article 165 of the Criminal Code, a necessary condition was the existence of an act of destruction. Zhang, as a porridge vendor, was unlikely to have much knowledge. Furthermore, according to the defendant's testimony, he hid the gun to seek a reward and had no intention of destroying evidence. Moreover, the article stated that the evidence must be of a criminal defendant, but at that time, the case had just occurred, and the police had not yet begun investigating, so there was no defendant. Therefore, the article was not applicable to the defendant's actions, and he could not be found guilty. He requested that the court declare him innocent. Furthermore, the defendant's family relied entirely on him for their livelihood, and he had been detained for a long time. Even if the court found him guilty, he requested that the court be lenient due to his ignorance. Prosecutor Tang requested that the law be applied. Judge Zhong then declared the debate closed and scheduled the verdict for 2 p.m. on the 30th.

Jiu Fu He Ji Construction Company Sues for Fraudulent Acquisition of Funds in Collusion with Foreigners - No Guandong Company Sugar Factory Exists - Credit Deposit of 3,000 Yuan Paid

Wang Dun'gen, a literary figure originally from Songjiang, formerly residing at No. 1, Beidaihe Road, was recently sued in a criminal case by Zhang Qingfu, the manager of the Jiu Fu He Ji Construction Company at No. 244 Tianjin Road, represented by lawyer Ling Qihong, to the First Special District Court for colluding with foreigners to defraud him of property, along with incidental civil claims. The complaint stated that the plaintiff was introduced to the defendant Wang Dun'gen by Liu Peilin. The defendant falsely claimed that a Japanese man, Amano Hachiro, had raised capital of 6 million yuan and was jointly operating the Guandong Company Sugar Factory with the Ministry of Finance of the National Government. He had been appointed as the Chinese manager and had designated the former National Sugar Factory building at No. 783 Taixing Road, Wusong, as the factory base. He commissioned the plaintiff to contract the renovation and repair work. The plaintiff, believing that the defendant was a reputable literary figure in Shanghai with high character, did not suspect him of any wrongdoing. On October 21st of last year, a contract was signed at the Nanjing Hotel with the Japanese Amano Hachiro, with lawyer Ling Qihong as a witness. The contract stated that construction would begin within three months and be completed within six months. The total cost was 236,500 yuan, to be paid in six installments. After the start of construction, 60,000 yuan would be paid within one week. The second, third, fourth, and fifth installments would each be 35,000 yuan, and the sixth installment would be 36,500 yuan. Article 10 of the contract stipulated that the plaintiff would first pay a credit deposit of 3,000 yuan, which would be returned upon completion. At that time, the plaintiff paid 3,000 yuan in cash to the defendant and Amano Hachiro at the Guandong Sugar Factory preparation office in the Tongsheng Foreign Firm building on Guangdong Road. However, it was later discovered that the so-called Guandong Company Sugar Factory was completely false, and the Ministry of Finance of the National Government had no joint venture with Amano Hachiro, nor did it intend to appoint Wang Dun'gen as the Chinese manager of the sugar factory. The defendant colluded with Amano Hachiro, using deceptive means to mislead the plaintiff into making the payment, which constitutes the crime of fraud under Article 339 of the Criminal Code. The plaintiff also filed an incidental civil claim, requesting the court to order the return of the credit deposit of 3,000 yuan and the statutory interest until the date of execution. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Dai Rongduo presided over the second criminal division and summoned the defendant Wang Dun'gen to his residence at No. 1, Beidaihe Road, but the summons could not be delivered because he had moved. The plaintiff Zhang Qingfu then came to the court to provide information about the case. His lawyer, Ling Qihong, stated that there was no Guandong Sugar Factory at all. The former National Sugar Factory was founded by Ma Yushan and others, but due to poor business and the Shanghai War, the building was almost destroyed by artillery fire. It was then mortgaged to the Japanese firm Fu He Yu Foreign Firm, owned by Ma Pingsan. Anyone wishing to visit could obtain a visitor's pass from the foreign firm. The defendant took advantage of this opportunity and visited the factory, paying the gatekeeper five yuan in legal tender, saying that if he brought friends in the future, he would ask them to be treated well. A few days later, the defendant accompanied the plaintiff to the factory. At that time, the defendant instructed the plaintiff on how to renovate and repair the factory, as if he were the owner. The plaintiff, unaware of the deception, was defrauded. Judge Dai, noting that the defendant had not arrived, ordered the postponement of the hearing to the afternoon of November 6th and issued a supplementary summons for the defendant Wang Dun'gen to appear in court for questioning.

Forging Letters to Entrust Carrying of Legal Tender - Scheming to Defraud 1,200 Yuan - Taking Advantage of Gu Xilang's Reputation - Public Prosecution Requires Summoning Witnesses for Investigation

Gu Xilang from Chongming, who has been working as a letter carrier at the Chongming Shipping Bureau, has a good reputation. Many Chongming merchants often entrust him to carry money and goods. Sha Cailang, a tea server at the Gongxing Fabric Shop in Qinbuli, Old Matou Road, Nanshi, and a customer named Song Ruihe conspired to find out where Gu kept his money so that they could steal it, as he often carried large sums of money. They found out that there was a Song Tianlun in Chongming County, and Song Tianlun Shen Zhuang in Shanghai, who buys and sells goods on behalf of customers. Song Ruihe forged a letter from the Chongming Song Tianlun's main store, asking Shen Zhuang to entrust Gu Xilang to carry 1,200 yuan in legal tender to Chongming to settle accounts. Song Tianlun Shen Zhuang, unaware of the forgery, immediately handed over the money. Song Ruihe, knowing that the letter had arrived and the money had been handed over, immediately ordered Sha Cailang to falsely claim that the Gongxing Fabric Shop had money to transport to Chongming, tricking Gu Xilang into going to the fabric shop. Gu, unaware of the deception, put the 1,200 yuan in a small wooden box and took it to the Gongxing Fabric Shop, placing it temporarily on the table while he contacted the accounting office. Unexpectedly, the shop had no such order. When Gu turned around, the box had disappeared. Realizing that he had been tricked, he reported the matter to the Nanshi Branch, who arrested Sha Cailang and interrogated him. Sha confessed that Song Ruihe had conceived the plan, forged a letter from Song Tianlun's main store asking to exchange for cash, sent it to Song Tianlun Shen Zhuang, and, after seeing Gu Xilang put the money in the box, colluded with two Shandong men on the night of October 8th to commit the theft. The branch, considering Song's elaborate and unprecedented scheme, and discovering that he was a major swindler with tens of thousands of yuan in assets, immediately dispatched a detective team to arrest Song and hand him over to the Public Security Bureau, which transferred him to the local court for detention. Gu Xilang also hired lawyer Shi Qinghua to file a private prosecution and an incidental civil claim. Yesterday, Judge Yu opened the court to hear the case. According to lawyer Shi, the civil part of the case had been settled by Song Ruihe's family, and he requested that the civil part be withdrawn, but he requested a trial for the criminal part. Judge Yu ordered that the details of the theft and the circumstances of the arrest should be investigated further by summoning witnesses and questioning the investigating detectives. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Continued Report on the Overturned Minhang Ferry - Details of the Deceased and Survivors

Around 11 a.m. the day before yesterday, the Luo A'gou ferry in Minhang Town, south of Shanghai, capsized due to strong winds. In addition to the dozen or so people rescued on the spot, more than 20 passengers were not rescued and tragically drowned. This was briefly reported in yesterday's newspaper. Further details from the investigation are as follows: Luo A'gou, 44 years old, lived in Luo Family Pond, south of the river. He had been a boatman for years. Since the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction's Highway Administration built a ferry in Minhang Town in the fall of the year before last, business had been slow, and Luo sold his ferry and sought other employment. Recently, he rented a private boat from Jiang Chunquan (34 years old) of Jiang Family Net Ferry, north of Minhang, and partnered with Jiang to continue ferrying passengers back and forth across the Huangpu River in Minhang Town. They charged only two copper coins per person, four coins less than the ferry, so many villagers were tempted by the cheaper fare. However, there were no limits, making it easy to cause accidents. Around 11 a.m. the day before yesterday, Luo and Jiang carried more than 40 passengers from the south bank of the river (opposite Minhang). As they reached the center of the river, they suddenly encountered strong winds, and the ferry turned from side to side and capsized instantly. All the passengers fell into the river. The water police patrol boat spotted them and quickly ordered a small ferry boat to rush to the rescue. They rescued 15 passengers from the water, including Wang Jiacai, Wang Changfu, Wu Youniu from Fengxian, and the boat owners Luo and Jiang. The rest drowned. Water police chief Zhang Jingqing and special agent team leader Wang Xingzhen ordered all patrol boats and hired five net boats to assist the water police in searching the Huangpu River. They recovered the bodies of Li Yishou, 51 years old, and Zhu Yunpu, 40 years old, who lived in the 2nd Bao, 8th Household of Zhugang Township, Fengxian. In the afternoon, the Shanghai Local Court sent prosecutor Lei and coroner Shen to the scene for inspection. They ordered the bodies to be handed over to Li Ruan, the wife of the deceased Li, and Zhu Lu, the wife of the deceased Zhu, for collection and burial. Yesterday, they recovered the bodies of Wang Ziqing, 56 years old, from the east of Xinqiao River; Pan A'shi, from Nandabqiao, age unknown; Li Rujin, 27 years old, and He A'tu, 10 years old, both from Zhugang Township; He Chenggen, 29 years old, and Wang Guansheng, 42 years old, both from Dingqiao Township; and Wang Wang, 20 years old, from Nandabqiao. All seven bodies, male and female, were claimed by their families for burial. Those who have not yet been recovered have been reported by their families to the 1st sub-district police station of the Fengxian County Public Security Bureau, including Chen Chunxiang, Ruan Jincai, Li Jingen, Li Zhu, Zhang Jinsong, Lu Botian, Zhu Jihai, A Kunsheng from Zhugang Township, and Ma Jinsheng and Fei Hai from Dingqiao Township. The north and south banks of the Huangpu River were filled with wails, a truly unbearable scene. The boat owners Luo A'gou and Jiang Chunquan, who caused the accident, are currently detained at the 1st District of the Water Police Station, awaiting a formal document to be sent to the court for trial.

The court reviewed the report and briefly questioned the defendants, then approved the postponement and ordered a joint trial with Dai Jinf on the 28th. The defendants were remanded in custody. The detectives handling the case discovered that the woman who pretended to rent the house, Xiang Qiumo, 25 years old, from Shaoxing, lived at No. 6, Lane 69, Jing'an Temple Road. She is currently under arrest by the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau and has been sent to the Shanghai Local Court for detention. Yesterday, Detective Shen Jinshu went to transfer Xiang Qiumo to the case, and she will be sent to the Second Special District Court today for a joint trial. Some of the stolen goods from the home of Sun Shichang, assistant manager of the Zhenfeng Cotton Mill, have been recovered. They are currently investigating and interrogating the criminals to recover the remaining stolen goods and firearms.

Mrs. Hu Xie Angered and Attempted Suicide - Swallowed Thirty-Seven Needles - Doctors Say Her Condition is Critical - Suffering from Abdominal Pain and Restlessness

Hu Xie, a 23-year-old woman from Yangzhou, who lives at No. 20, Weixinli, at the intersection of Pingliang Road and Taopeng Road, swallowed thirty-seven flower needles wrapped in paper in an attempt to kill herself after arguing with her husband yesterday morning around 7 a.m. Around 6 p.m. yesterday, she was discovered to be suffering from abdominal pain and restlessness. She was immediately taken by car to Tongren Hospital for treatment. After examination, the hospital determined that her condition was very critical and her life was in danger.

The Death of Li Xiangying: Two Men Vie for Her Wealth, Exposing a Scandal - Lu Shande's Affair with an Elderly Woman for Money - Li Mingsong Claims Marital Status Pending Proof

Li Mingsong from Hangzhou (also known as Li Hongnian, 59 years old) has been running the Laoda Fang Knife Shop at No. 276 Wuchang Road. His wife, Li Xiangying (also known as Li Suyan, 51 years old), whom he married 30 years ago, lived with him at the shop. Li Mingsong once apprenticed under Jin Qinji of the Guangdong Triad Society. A Ningbo man named Lu Shande (29 years old) was also Jin's disciple, through which he became acquainted with Li Mingsong. An affair developed, and Li Mingsong allowed Lu to live in the Laoda Fang Knife Shop, which he has been doing for over two years. On the 18th of last month, Li Xiangying became seriously ill. At the time, she told her husband, Li Mingsong, that she had a China Bank savings account with 1,000 yuan in it, kept in a box, and handed him the key. On the 7th of this month, her illness worsened, and she was expected to die. Li Mingsong discussed funeral arrangements with Lu Shande, leading to a dispute, and Lu snatched the key that Li had given Li Mingsong. On the 9th, Li Xiangying died, and the funeral arrangements were jointly handled by Li Mingsong and Lu. Over 200 yuan was spent on funeral expenses, all borrowed by Lu. On the 19th of this month, Li Mingsong learned from the China Bank that the 1,000 yuan had been withdrawn by Lu. He confronted Lu on the afternoon of the previous day, but Lu presented two documents. Since Li was illiterate, Lu read the contents of the two documents to him. They required Li to acknowledge that the Laoda Fang Knife Shop had been transferred to Lu and a newspaper advertisement to that effect. Li refused and reported the matter to the Hongkou Police Station at 8:50 PM the previous night. Detective Zhang Liansheng and others arrested Lu. Lu admitted to the affair with Li Xiangying and stated that he was with the elderly woman because she had some savings. He also admitted to withdrawing the China Bank deposit, stating that he deposited 400 yuan with his master Jin Qinji, returned 290 yuan to various creditors, and used the remainder for funeral expenses. He also claimed that Li Xiangying had transferred the Laoda Fang Knife Shop to him for 500 yuan. The detectives went to Jin's residence at No. 1337 Wuchang Road and recovered the 400 yuan. Yesterday morning, they escorted Lu to the Fifth Criminal Court of the Special District Court. The police lawyer Jiang Baolian explained the situation. Due to the complexity of the case, further investigation was required, so he requested permission to detain Lu for one week for further interrogation. When questioned, Lu Shande claimed that the deceased, Zhang Li, was his adopted mother and had been living with him and his 15-year-old son in the Laoda Fang Knife Shop. He stated that the plaintiff, Li Mingsong, did not live there and ran another knife shop on Caishi Road and was not Zhang Li's husband. Li Mingsong claimed that he and Li Xiangying were indeed husband and wife, and he still had a 77-year-old mother-in-law alive. Judge Zhan Liangce reviewed the statements and ordered Lu Shande to be detained for one week, and ordered Li Mingsong to provide evidence proving that he and Li Xiangying were formally married.

Mammoth Production by the Research Department of the Bank of China - Publication of the National Banking Yearbook

The Economic Research Department of the Bank of China's General Administration has consistently spared no effort in economic research, and the various books it has compiled have made significant contributions to economic research. Previously, recognizing the lack of complete and systematic records and statistics on China's banking industry, it began compiling and printing the National Banking Yearbook in 1934. After its publication, it was widely praised by all sectors as the only reliable reference for studying the banking industry. Since the publication of the second edition last July, it has been engaged in the third investigation and compilation, which took nearly a year to complete. The compilation methods have also been greatly reformed to ensure accuracy, completeness, and convenience in inspection and application. According to the person in charge of the department, this is the third edition of the yearbook since its publication. After the publication of the previous two editions, experts and banking authorities at home and abroad were consulted for corrections in order to meet practical needs. Various sectors generously provided valuable suggestions, either with excessive praise or detailed guidance on the compilation direction, providing strict criticism. The department studied these opinions and incorporated them. Therefore, the second edition had some supplements, and this year's edition has further reformed the compilation to fulfill the original intention of compiling the yearbook. The entire book is divided into three parts: upper, middle, and lower. The upper part provides a systematic description of the origin and current status of China's banking industry and the changes in 1935, and also provides a detailed analysis of the business overview of the most recent four years. At the same time, it also publishes the brief history, current status, and the most recent two years' balance sheet and profit and loss of each bank. The middle part focuses on the investigation of the financial situation in various regions, providing detailed records of the evolution and current status of various local silver and money businesses, pawnshops, warehouses, and financial market conditions. The lower part classifies and statistically analyzes the financial market conditions, bill exchange, and the business overview of national banks in the most recent four years, so that readers can have a clear overview. In addition, it also includes the current banking laws and regulations, the regulations of various banks, annual reports, diaries, banking essays, directory indexes, etc., which are essential references for those engaged in the banking industry and those studying banking. The entire book has more than 2,300 pages, totaling more than 4 million words. It is printed in regular script using rice-colored Daolin paper and bound in a beautifully leather-covered volume. In order to achieve widespread dissemination, the price has been specially reduced from eight yuan to six yuan, reducing the burden on readers by 25%.

Municipal Finance Bureau - Announces Brokerage Regulations - Revised Regulations for Brokerage Business in This City - Detailed Rules for Levying Brokerage Tax

The Municipal Finance Bureau previously drafted revisions to the Shanghai Municipal Brokerage Business Regulations and the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau's Detailed Rules for Levying Brokerage Tax and submitted them to the Municipal Government for referral to the Ministry of Finance for approval. The Ministry of Finance has now revised them and submitted them to the Executive Yuan for record-keeping, and has notified the Municipal Government to instruct the bureau to comply. The full text of the regulations is recorded as follows:

Revised Shanghai Municipal Brokerage Business Regulations

Article 1: The term "brokerage" in these regulations refers to any business that manages goods and passengers, and collects commissions for buying and selling on behalf of customers. Article 2: Anyone opening a brokerage within the city limits must comply with these regulations, register with the Finance Bureau to obtain a brokerage registration certificate, and pay the following taxes: (A) Registration Tax (paid once when obtaining the certificate) (B) Business Tax (paid annually). Article 3: Applicants for a brokerage registration certificate must specify the following items in their application and provide a guarantee from a reputable store (or pay a security deposit of 200 to 500 yuan according to their grade), and attach a brief description of the brokerage's organization and tasks. After the Finance Bureau verifies and approves the application, a certificate will be issued for operation. 1. Brand name, 2. Business address, 3. Goods brokered, 4. Tax level, 5. Capital and annual sales amount or brokerage commission income, 6. Name, age, place of origin, and address of the brokerage operator. Article 4: The brokerage registration certificate is issued by the Finance Bureau and filled out by the four tax collection offices in the East, South, West, and North districts. The taxes payable are collected by the competent tax collection office in accordance with the regulations. Article 5: Brokerage registration certificates are divided into long-term and short-term. New certificates must be exchanged upon expiration. (1) Long-term certificate (valid for five years from the date of issuance) (2) Short-term certificate (valid for one year from the date of issuance). Article 6: The registration tax for short-term certificates is based on the following rates: A. Prosperous Area: First Class: 60 yuan per household, Second Class: 120 yuan per household, Third Class: 80 yuan per household, Fourth Class: 40 yuan per household. B. Remote Area: First Class: 80 yuan per household, Second Class: 60 yuan per household, Third Class: 40 yuan per household, Fourth Class: 20 yuan per household. Article 7: The distinction between prosperous and remote areas for long-term certificates is based on the following criteria: A. Prosperous Area: City districts and city areas of this city. B. Remote Area: All townships in this city. If the market conditions of the location of the business within the scope of the aforementioned regulations are significantly different, the Finance Bureau may investigate and approve adjustments. Article 8: The registration tax for short-term certificates is based on the following rates: First Class: 40 yuan per household, Second Class: 24 yuan, Third Class: 16 yuan, Fourth Class: 10 yuan. Article 9: The registration tax is paid once upon obtaining the certificate, according to the grade listed in the brokerage goods list. Regardless of whether it is a long-term or short-term certificate, each certificate is limited to brokering one type of goods and may not concurrently broker other types. If it is found that other goods are being brokered concurrently, an order must be issued to obtain a short-term certificate before operation is permitted. Article 10: If items not listed in the goods list are discovered, the Finance Bureau may investigate the nature of the items and classify them into a certain type of goods, or establish another type of goods to determine the grade for issuing the certificate. Article 11: The annual business tax for long-term certificates is based on the following rates: A. Prosperous Area: First Class: 25 yuan per household, Second Class: 17 yuan per household, Third Class: 10 yuan per household, Fourth Class: 5 yuan per household. B. Remote Area: First Class: 12 yuan per household, Second Class: 9 yuan per household, Third Class: 6 yuan per household, Fourth Class: 4 yuan per household. Article 12: The business tax for long-term certificates, in addition to the first year's tax which should be paid at the same time as the registration tax, the subsequent annual business tax should be paid within one month from the date of the original certificate's issuance. If the regulatory deadline is exceeded, a late fee of 5% of the tax amount will be added for less than one month, 10% for less than two months, and 20% for less than three months. If payment is still not made after three months, the certificate may be revoked, operation is not permitted, and the full year's tax will still be collected. Article 13: The annual business tax for short-term certificates is based on the following rates: First Class: 10 yuan per household, Second Class: 7.5 yuan, Third Class: 5 yuan, Fourth Class: 2.5 yuan. (Incomplete)

Special Publication for the Presentation and Naming Ceremony of Airplanes for Chiang Kai-shek's Birthday

On the Occasion of Chairman Chiang's Fiftieth Birthday

Our President of the Executive Yuan and Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, Mr. Chiang Kai-shek, was born in the summer of the 9th month of the Dinghai year, twenty-five years before the Republic (October 29th), marking his fiftieth birthday. As the Book of Songs says, "The mountains bring forth spirits, giving birth to Fu and Shen. As with Shen, so with Fu, a shield for the four states, an announcement to the four directions." Mr. Chiang embodies both Shen and Fu in one person, and his great achievements for the country, embroidered robes, and chants of praise, extend far beyond a shield and an announcement. The three hundred poems of the Book of Songs express emotions and character, created by poets to influence their superiors, collected by the Grand Master to present to the court, to observe the customs of the people, and to examine the changes in the world. The essential principle is to hope for longevity and to create a noble person. Out of love and respect, people invariably offer small gifts, saying, "This is a robe for the duke," or "This is a fur coat for the duke," offering them in private. "Carrying on military achievements, offering boars to the public," offering them in public. "Make this spring wine, to bring long life," "Ascend to the court, raise the rhinoceros horn cup, ten thousand years of boundless life," offering gifts and then extending words of praise, with heartfelt intentions for the benefit of the people. The intimacy of friends, reciprocating with peach and plum, is indeed fitting human sentiment. But as for "showing me the way, virtuous sounds are clear," seeing the people as not frivolous, joyous guests feast, and in between, they must blow the reed pipe and beat the reed organ, carrying baskets to present, calmly and communicating, convinced in their hearts, following the law, and emulating. Therefore, the Lesser Odes say, "The noble person is to be followed and emulated." The emotions between superiors and subordinates are connected, and the harmony and joy are not something that ordinary private matters can describe in words. The Book of Songs says, "The road to Zhou is like a whetstone, its straightness like an arrow," speaking of the righteousness of the way. It also says, "The hurried travelers, always fearing they will not make it, six reins like silk, galloping and driving," speaking of the king's affairs taking precedence. It also says, "Coming from the secluded valley, connecting to the tall trees, chirping its song, seeking its friend's voice," speaking of those who seek friends can rise from obscurity to clarity, from humility to elevation. Therefore, the poem "Heaven Protects" praises, "May you have many benefits, with nothing not being plentiful, may you have abundant grain, with nothing not being appropriate." The people are simple, using food and drink daily, and the commentary says "Heaven protects, the lower reports to the upper." The respect of the lower for the upper comes from the heart, daily food and drink are all due to the virtue of the upper, and there is no wasted effort, then the foundation of blessing is established. So, how will colleagues offer their blessings to Mr. Chiang on his birthday? Asking the crowd, "Like birds reforming, like pheasants flying, clearly correct, the noble person is at peace, dwelling and living, laughing and talking," what is it? "You dukes and lords, leisure has no end, be careful in your leisure," what is the path? "Your peaceful journey, not even taking a break, your two journeys, not even greasing your chariot," how do you reach the goal? The crowd all said, "Five-cornered beams and shafts, moving rings and straps, setting up this flag, building that banner, those fluttering flags, why not waver, fluttering turtledoves, hurrying and galloping, bestowing on me a hundred strings of cowries, one morning to repay them." The crane speaks of longevity. Is it in this that they offer longevity to Mr. Chiang? Is it in this? Truly a noble person, unfolding and achieving greatly. Based on the poems, let this be the opening, initiator (initiator titles, omitted due to space limitations)

Donation of Funds by Various Organs Under the Municipal Government for the Purchase of Airplanes to Celebrate Mr. Chiang's Birthday

On October 31st of this year, we joyfully celebrate the fiftieth birthday of the President of the Executive Yuan and Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, Mr. Chiang Kai-shek. Reflecting on Mr. Chiang's timely virtue and surpassing achievements, for ten years our people have been able to live and work in peace, undisturbed by war, all thanks to his beneficence. This year coincides with his birthday, and all sectors of the city, in order to repay his special achievements and to accord with public opinion, first advocated raising funds to purchase airplanes as a birthday gift. As the highest administrative organ in Shanghai, our government should take the lead to set an example. In June, we formulated the Measures for Donating Funds by Public Servants, Military Police, and Servants of Various Organs Under the Government for the Purchase of Airplanes to Celebrate Mr. Chiang's Birthday, and issued a circular to deduct and collect donations. This is the sincere intention of all the officials, soldiers, police, and servants of the government to express their respect and love for the leader and to support the country. The original measures are listed below:

Public servants, military police, and servants should all deduct and donate according to the following standards, for the months of July and August of this year:

A. For those with a monthly original salary of 49 yuan or less, deduct 2%.

B. For those with a monthly original salary of 50 yuan to 99 yuan, deduct 5%.

C. For those with a monthly original salary of 100 yuan to 199 yuan, deduct 6%.

D. For those with a monthly original salary of 200 yuan to 299 yuan, deduct 7%.

E. For those with a monthly original salary of 300 yuan to 399 yuan, deduct 8%.

F. For those with a monthly original salary of 400 yuan to 499 yuan, deduct 9%.

G. For those with a monthly original salary of 500 yuan or more, deduct 10%.

Those with special office expenses must also deduct donations according to the above percentage standards.

In July and August, the government collected donations from all organs, which have been delivered to the Shanghai Committee for the Purchase of Airplanes to Celebrate Mr. Chiang's Birthday as scheduled. Now, on the occasion of the Shanghai presentation of the airplane naming ceremony, we record the entire process of the government's deduction of funds for the purchase of airplanes as above.

Ningbo Fellow-Townsmen Association in Shanghai: A Few Words Regarding This Purchase of Aircraft for Birthday Greetings

The giant wheel of the times advances rapidly like flowing water. Everything relies on the omnipotence of science, reaching the pinnacle of its realm. Humanity's methods of mutual slaughter in war have evolved from two-dimensional forms to three-dimensional ones. The greatness of iron birds soaring high above, their destructive and attacking power, has long been recognized by military strategists. Therefore, all aggressive nations in the world with vaulting ambitions seek to expand their air forces as tools for invasion. Those small and weak nations that are likely to be invaded also spare no effort to substantially enrich their air forces, using them as the foundation of national defense and for necessary self-defense.

The simplicity of our nation's aviation equipment and the inherent weakness of our national defense are undeniable. Now, great calamity is approaching. Once it erupts, won't the lives of our 490 million people become sacrifices under the giant bombs of the ferocious imperialists' planes? Won't our ancient country with 5,000 years of history instantly become a field of rubble under the brutal bombing of the violent aggressors? The tear stains of September 18th have not yet dried, and the tragic scenes of January 28th are still vivid in our minds. If we are unwilling to lose our nation and our homes, then we must use the power of the entire nation to enrich our aviation equipment!

Our nation, with its 490 million people, has already deeply tasted the pain of brutal bombing by aggressors, knowing that rudimentary aviation equipment is insufficient for survival in the present world. Therefore, the China Aviation Association was established the year before last, and at the same time, a campaign to raise funds for purchasing aircraft to save the nation was launched to aid national defense. Our association's members, with patriotic enthusiasm, also organized an Aviation Salvation Fundraising Committee to fulfill the duties of citizens. The results were extremely good. People in Shanghai should remember the grand occasion when the Ningbo aircraft and various sectors held naming ceremonies at the same time.

Chairman Chiang is dedicated to the Party and the nation, his hard work and great achievements are our only leader. This year, for his 50th birthday celebration, we organized the Ningbo Fellow-Townsmen in Shanghai Aircraft Purchase for Birthday Greetings Fundraising Committee, electing Yu Qiaqing, Zhu Shoumei, and Jin Tingsun as chairman and vice-chairmen, and Zhi Xiao'an, Xu Zhichan, Zhang Jiguang, Yu Zuoting, Wu Daoting, Yuan Ludeng, and Zhu Meixian as standing committee members, with Zhang Shenzhi, Niao Yaqin, and Mao Heyuan as general managers. After its establishment, a dinner meeting was held at 82 Henry Road to discuss methods. In addition to the committee members, there were more than 50 people present, including Liu Hongsheng, Zhang Yongni, Sun Hegao, Wang Boyuan, Zhou Xiangsheng, Qin Runqing, and Sun Hengfu. At that time, everyone believed that the Chairman's birthday was the birthday of our Republic of China, and that purchasing aircraft to strengthen national defense was indeed the only key to praying for the eternal life of our nation. It was unanimously advocated to raise 100,000 yuan, independently purchase aircraft, and present it to the government as a birthday gift for the Chairman. Over the past few months, we have received enthusiastic support from our fellow-townsmen, and the great cause has been successfully completed. Do we want to wish Chairman Chiang longevity, or China longevity? Do we want to wish longevity to Chairman Chiang alone, or to the 450 million people? We fervently hope that the world's weak and small nations will unanimously respond to the aggressors' weapons with their own weapons, and to the aggressors' air force with their own national defense air force, so that the aggressors will know to restrain themselves, and the weak and small nations can survive forever in the world.

The Process of Fundraising and Purchasing Aircraft for Birthday Greetings by Students in Collective Training

Since the municipal government advocated the method of dedicating aircraft for birthday greetings, people from far and wide followed suit. The officers and students in our collective training are deeply enthusiastic about this grand event! Through the entire body of officers and students in the collective training headquarters, they initiated the purchase of an aircraft named "Shanghai Collective Training Students," and the method of raising funds was: starting with all the officers and students saving on food and clothing to accumulate a fund of more than 3,000 yuan, and then organizing a "Collective Training Students Aircraft Fundraising Committee" to engage in solicitation, stipulating that each collective training student would donate 10 yuan or appropriately reduce the amount based on their family's circumstances. The donation amount for officers and instructors was not limited. However, small streams are difficult to gather into a great effect, and hearts were willing but strength was lacking. Therefore, the remaining amount was turned to colleagues outside who care for military training and are enthusiastic about saving the nation to continue fundraising. Furthermore, students from various teams were mobilized in a rotating manner, raising 43,038.97 yuan in legal tender, for a total of 46,954.104 yuan in legal tender raised before and after. The remaining amount has been planned for fundraising by Commander Song and others in conjunction with the Aircraft Purchase Birthday Greetings Commemoration Committee. It is noted that the current collective training officers and students number only over 5,000, and they were able to raise nearly 50,000 yuan in a short period with the assistance of various sectors. This is due to the passion of patriotism and the sincerity of faith in the leader, which led to success, and the ability to inspire the enthusiasm and faith of various sectors to create this unprecedented grand event. This is due to the great achievements and virtues of our Chairman! As the grand celebration approaches, the fundraising method and the process are briefly described above to record a general overview. (Military Training Committee manuscript)

The Process of Fundraising for Aviation Donations by the Hotel Industry Association

— Sun Qiuping

(1) The Motivating Factor: Since the Shanghai War, the Chinese people have had a deep understanding of the power and cruelty of the air force. The hotel industry colleagues, after reflecting on the pain, believed that to save the country and ensure survival, it is necessary to build an air force. To build an air force, the people must assist the government and work together. At that time, Yao Songnian of Shen Tai Hotel and Zhou Songxi of Weisheng Hotel, two committee members, first suggested that the hotel industry should raise funds to purchase aircraft. The main idea of their proposal was: Currently, the people of aggressive countries are enthusiastically assisting their governments in raising funds to purchase aircraft. How can the people of invaded countries ignore their own demise? We should rise up quickly to fulfill our responsibilities as citizens. If the businesses of all hotels in the city can extract and collect a percentage, it will surely accumulate to be able to purchase warplanes. If all industries nationwide hear the news and follow suit, then the power of the hotel industry's purchase of aircraft to promote the response of all industries nationwide in saving the country and ensuring survival will be significant! Therefore, they specially requested that a general meeting be convened to make a public decision. This was the initial motivation for the hotel industry to raise funds to purchase aircraft.

(2) The Determined Method: After the hotel industry colleagues had the motivation to raise funds to purchase aircraft, they painstakingly planned the fundraising method. On May 18 of the second year, the Shanghai Aviation Association sent a letter to this association, supporting aviation movement and making every effort to donate. The 12th plenary meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committee was immediately convened, and the Aviation Association sent Zhang Yuliang as a representative to attend. After deliberation, it was decided (A) to ask Representative Zhang to convey to the Chief Commander that the public association should be substantially supported in organizing and improving so that it can be collected, (B) to appoint committee members Yao Songnian, Zhou Songxi, Sun Qiuping, Gao Weifu, Xu Wenzhao, Xu Mengyuan, Yan Rongqing, and Zhang Yichen to visit Chief Commander Wu and negotiate progress, (C) to pass the Shanghai Hotel Industry Method for Collecting Aviation and National Salvation Donations as follows: (1) The Shanghai Hotel Industry Association has formulated this method for the purpose of assisting the Aviation Association in promoting aviation salvation funds. (2) Each hotel shall add 5% to the room rate as an aviation and national salvation donation. (3) Each hotel shall collect the aviation and national salvation donation once a month and hand it over to the China Aviation Association. (4) Each hotel shall issue a receipt to the passengers for the aviation and national salvation donation collected. (5) Each hotel shall post the method of collecting the aviation and national salvation donation in each room so that passengers are aware. (6) The collection of the aviation and national salvation donation by the hotel industry shall be limited to raising 200,000 yuan. (7) The China Aviation Association shall print joint receipt forms for collecting the hotel industry aviation donation and distribute them to each hotel. (8) The China Aviation Association may send personnel to investigate the collection situation. If there are any malpractices, they shall be punished according to law. (9) The China Aviation Association shall announce the amount of aviation and national salvation donation income from the hotel industry every month. (10) This method shall be submitted to the municipal government for approval and implementation.

(3) The Fundraising Process: (A) Beginning of Collection: After the collection method was approved by the municipal government, there was a thorough preparatory work in the middle, and the situation of hotels throughout the city was investigated, divided into five grades: special, A, B, C, and D, and after preparation, the collection began on April 15 of the third year. The Aviation Association was requested to send additional personnel to be responsible for investigation. However, at the beginning of the collection, there were many obstacles. At the beginning, there was a misunderstanding by the police, which almost caused the work to come to a standstill. (B) The Situation of Negotiations: After the hotels started collecting aviation donations, the standing bureaus of the two concessions did not understand the purpose of the collection, causing misunderstandings and preventing the collection. As a result, most hotels should have announced a stop and requested negotiations. This association immediately requested the Aviation Association to submit a protest to the municipal government. After the municipal government negotiated the result, the misunderstanding was resolved. On June 25, the Aviation Association convened representatives of major hotels at the YMCA in Baixianqiao to discuss the continuation of the rectification method. Chief Commander Ying and the Chamber of Commerce's _ wheeled, successively pointed _, and immediately decided the method of merit collection as follows:

1. Uniformly continue collection on July 10,

2. Request the municipal government to reissue an announcement for guidance,

3. All hotels, regardless of special A, B, C, and D, shall collect. If any hotel is unwilling to collect, it shall voluntarily pay a certain amount to show its support,

4. The aviation donation for special A, B, and C grades shall still be deducted by 5%, and the D grade shall be 3 yuan, also according to the original method,

5. Please send personnel from the China Aviation Association to investigate day by day. For hotels that do not collect, please also advise them separately. (C) Organizing a Fundraising Association: Since the decision to continue collection was made, the wait-and-see attitude of a small number of colleagues still inevitably affected it. This association organized a Fundraising Committee in September of the same year, electing hotel industry magnates to be dedicated to fundraising work. The list of fundraising committee members is as follows: Ni Xianting, Chen Wenda, Gao Weifu, Liu Qirun, Xu Mengyuan, Zhou Songxi, Yao Songnian, Yan Rongqing, Zhan Wenxi, Li Wenrui, Shen Changgeng, Xu Xinquan, Zhang Renliang, Li J眉mei, Gu J眉mei, Xu Wenzhao, Zhao Quansheng, Zou Xieqing, Zhang Qiyuan, Yao Zhaoji, Wang Changgeng, Sun Qiuping, Zhou Xiangsheng, and Ren Yueer. Chen Tianyin and other 25 people, at that time, each fundraising committee member was assigned to fundraising work, and each hotel was grateful for the public friendship and private relations, and all accepted the advice. By this point, the foundation of the hotel industry aviation donation was laid, and the official collection began. (D) Police Interference Again: In March of this year, the political department of the French Concession Police Department fined Da Hu, Asia, Dafang, Guangtailai, Ping An, Changjiang, and Taian Trading Stations for collecting aviation donations, and stopped the collection. At the same time, the police officers of major hotels in the Public Concession also collected donation books and receipts. After this association forwarded the request to the Aviation Association and the Municipal Government for negotiation, all sectors of this city supported this association. As a result, the police side also knew that the patriotic movement of our people should not be overly suppressed, so they indicated that they would no longer obstruct those who voluntarily donate. This association then advised colleagues to continue the collection. (4) Conclusion: From the above-mentioned facts, the difficulties encountered by this association in collecting the hotel industry aviation donation are: First, the colleagues failed to join the association unanimously, resulting in the preparation and implementation being more time-consuming and laborious. Second, the misunderstanding of the concession authorities caused the colleagues to hesitate and wait and see. Again, the decline of business, the mutual price reduction and competition among colleagues almost made it impossible for the colleagues to maintain their own survival. The impact on the collection of aviation donations is self-evident. In addition to devoting itself to fundraising work, this association also planned to unify discounts and stabilize room rates as indirect assistance. Fortunately, under the leadership of Chief Commander Wu Tiecheng and General Manager Gu Dachao of the Aviation Association, and the enthusiastic support of people from all walks of life, we have overcome difficulties and completed initial results, so that the Hotel Industry No. 1 aircraft can soar in the sky. But we will never be satisfied with the Hotel Industry aircraft, and we sincerely hope that the success of the Hotel Industry team will lead to the naming of the Hotel Industry aircraft, which can be used as a touchstone for other industries, that the hotel industry can overcome difficulties and purchase warplanes, and other industries can also overcome difficulties, hearing the news and following suit, and will surely catch up later. If one industry is like this, and it is extended to all industries in the country, then the contribution to saving the country and ensuring survival will be immeasurable.

The Process of Purchasing and Dedicating the "Grains and Cereals" Aircraft - Shanghai Grains, Cereals, Oil Cakes Trade Association

Chairman Chiang has devoted his efforts to the Party and the nation, defending the nation, securing internal stability, and resisting external aggression, establishing the country in an era of turmoil, working tirelessly day and night to save the people from fire and water. His great achievements and magnificent deeds will shine forever like the sun and moon. His great kindness and virtue will extend to the mountains and forests. Now, on the occasion of his 50th birthday, in the year of abundant harvests, with peace and prosperity throughout the world, the people are joyful and grateful, and should express their love and support, singing praises and offering blessings to wish him long life. Then the Shanghai Aircraft Purchase Fundraising Committee issued a notice to assist in the proceedings. The collection of donations on goods began on August 3, and they were submitted to the municipal committee one after another. During this preparation period, the members of this association went through consultations and did their best to work hard. The municipal committee guided the proceedings and assisted in time, which helped us even more. Today, the Shanghai Grains and Cereals aircraft is holding a naming ceremony at Longhua Flying Port. Chairman Gu Xin of this association and the representatives of all colleagues, Cai Yukun, Chen Ziyi, Zhu Zixiang, Chen Shide, He Quansheng, He Xianggu, Wu Zisheng, and Jiang Hongbin, will go to the site to participate in the grand ceremony. It is truly an unparalleled honor.
