Women's Special

How to Be a Woman in Extraordinary Times

— Wu Zizhen

The life of the nation has reached a critical juncture. How should our female compatriots awaken to fulfill the responsibility of self-salvation and national salvation? My opinion is that the following points must be considered:

First, Reform Our Hearts: We know that many female compatriots are very spirited and capable of independence, but it cannot be denied that many are doing or expecting to be appendages or toys of men! (Such as concubines and spouses whose unions are purely based on money and status.) To be a rational woman of extraordinary times, we must first eliminate this base mentality and immediately raise the banner of self-reliance and independence.

Second, Practice Frugality: We know that when war truly breaks out, the government needs not only weapons such as guns and cannons, but also a large amount of economic resources and food! And most of those who are appendages of men are due to their own excessive consumption. Therefore, if we want to be self-reliant and love the country, we should start with frugality ourselves.

Third, Shift Your Love's Focus: In general, young and promising women are often immersed in romantic dreams. Although there are many extremely valuable and noble stories among them, we cannot deny that love is a part of young people's lives. But if we make a rational critique with the interests of the country as a prerequisite, then we feel that their immersion is really a loss to the country! (Because the only people the country relies on are our young people, and the only ones who can take on the responsibility of struggle are our young people!) Therefore, although I acknowledge the nobility of love, I cannot acknowledge the supremacy of love! I do not advocate being intoxicated in the arms of a lover, dreaming of pathetic and moving dreams. I believe that women in extraordinary times should only encourage their lovers or husbands to be loyal to the country, or accompany their lovers and husbands to be loyal to the country! Women who excessively indulge in tenderness, causing men to become numb and the country to lose warriors, are truly shameful and guilty of the same crime as traitors! I hope that female compatriots who have lovers (or beloved husbands) can love the majority of compatriots with the love of a few people, and shift the focus of your love to the entire country and the entire nation!

Fourth, Strive to Study and Exercise: Studying can increase knowledge, and exercising can strengthen the body. After the outbreak of war, every citizen should contribute everything they have, and sacrifice their own lives and property without hesitation. But if their academic ability is insufficient or their physical strength is inadequate, they will inevitably want to sacrifice but be unable to, or sacrifice inappropriately! - But there is one point that everyone must understand: - Sacrifice does not only refer to direct sacrifice on the battlefield or in war. Providing rescue in the rear or replacing men's work is also a kind of sacrifice!

Women of the whole country! Female compatriots standing at the forefront of the times! You should quickly awaken and prepare to take on your own responsibilities, and with the spirit of establishing oneself and establishing others, and achieving oneself and achieving others, encourage those who are behind to work and sacrifice for the country together!

National Heroine

— Wen Feizi

Qin Liangyu was from Zhongzhou, Sichuan. She did not like to apply makeup. From a young age, she liked to ride horses and was good at archery. She often dressed as a man. Her husband was called Ma Qiancheng, and he was the Pacification Commissioner in Shigui, Sichuan. Once, there was a rebellion in Bozhou (now Zunyi, Guizhou). The situation was serious. She led 500 elite soldiers to help her husband quell the rebellion. This was a small display of her skills, and the people had already benefited greatly. Therefore, after Qiancheng died, his official position was taken over by her.

At that time, the Ming Dynasty's powerful enemy, the Manchus, attacked Liaodong from Manchuria, and the border defense was very tense. The government ordered Qin Liangyu to lead her troops to defend against the enemy. Her elder brother led the troops and set off first. Unfortunately, when he arrived at the Hun River (the name of a river in Liaoning), he died in battle there. Her younger brother was besieged by enemy troops and was in a critical situation. When Qin Liangyu arrived, she drove back the enemy troops and lifted the siege. People without courage and ability could not have done that.

When Liangyu returned to Sichuan, Chongqing was being tightly besieged by rebel troops again. She once again exerted her divine martial prowess and dispersed the enemy troops. Afterwards, the Chongqing government set up a feast to congratulate Liangyu on her achievements. This was such a glorious event!

However, people with ability are easily envied. There was a commander-in-chief named Li Weixin who saw Liangyu repeatedly making great achievements and was very jealous. Once, he was defeated in battle and returned to camp. Liangyu went to see him, but he refused to open the door. Therefore, Liangyu wrote a letter to the emperor saying, "Li Weixin, a six-foot-tall man, is jealous of a woman. He should feel ashamed to death when he thinks about it at night." This was truly a scolding that felt good. The emperor then issued an edict ordering all civil and military officials in Sichuan to treat Liangyu with respect and not to be suspicious of her. Our national heroine had won.

In the third year of Chongzhen, the border defense was alarmed again. Liangyu was ordered to move her troops. When the emperor saw that she was loyal to the country and not afraid of hardship, he summoned her to the platform and gave her four poems, with two lines inside: "There are not a few extraordinary men in the world, but who is willing to travel thousands of miles on the battlefield." In his words, he revealed infinite emotion, and Liangyu's loyalty and courage can be imagined.

Later, the bandit Zhang Xianzhong attacked Sichuan. The Sichuan authorities failed to adopt Liangyu's strategy, which led to the rampant banditry and no way to resist. Sichuan was ravaged by him, and the smoke was desolate, with nine out of ten houses empty. However, Shigui was never breached by the bandits, which was also the result of Liangyu and the people working together to resist. While the entire province was devastated, one side was clean. The name of the national heroine Qin Liangyu was known to everyone and became a national heroine admired by people throughout the ages.

Special Report by This Newspaper

Ms. Du Yufei's Thoughts on Touring Europe

— Huang Jiping

Hungarians are the most patriotic and can serve as our role models! German and Italian women are the most hardworking, providing equal service to men.

Following the closing of the Olympic Games, the nation felt a thousand sorrows and regrets, considering it a major stain on China's sporting history. Especially those in the sports world expressed their views and debated the matter. Although there is still no comprehensive plan for advancement, everyone has deeply awakened, realizing it's never too late to mend the fold and catch up quickly, determined not to fail forever. Frankly speaking, as a weak nation like ours, we lag behind in everything, let alone sports, which is a common matter! A few days ago, I met Ms. Du Yufei, the principal of the China Women's Physical Education Normal School, who accompanied the sports delegation to Europe this time. She heard and saw a lot, and was deeply moved. I presented some opinions, and she responded to each one. Below is a quick sketch of the conversation:

"What was the itinerary and route of the sports delegation's trip to Europe?"

"The delegation consisted of 37 people, including eight women. We left the country at the end of June and returned to Shanghai on October 3, spending 99 days on the road. We passed through nine countries, including Italy, Germany, Austria, Hungary, Sweden, Denmark, Czechoslovakia, Egypt, and India. We stayed in Germany for a longer time, and the rest were just brief sightseeing tours, like watching flowers from horseback."

"What are your impressions of this year's Olympics?"

"The press has reported extensively on the various aspects of the Games. Now, I would like to offer a few personal impressions: Overseas, I felt that our national spirit was very poor. The people of other countries acted with complete discipline, prioritizing the country over the individual. We were ashamed of our inferiority. The main reasons for the delegation's failure were: first, we lacked physical strength and sufficient nutrition; second, we lacked long-term training; third, we lacked on-the-spot experience. For example, in basketball, our technique was not bad, but the players were flustered and didn't know what to do, resulting in a disastrous loss that far exceeded expectations; fourth, the athletes' lives were too undisciplined, and too few people could abide by the rules; fifth, everyone lacked a sense of responsibility and disregarded the country's reputation. For example, when they went abroad, the athletes always complained about being unaccustomed to the food, and one got sick, then another, keeping the doctors busy and causing a lot of jokes, which is hard to put into words. When they returned home, they were all cheerful and didn't feel any remorse for their failure! What do you think? Let bygones be bygones. In the future, we should work hard. The next Games will be held in Japan. To talk about winning the championship might be too extravagant. I advocate that in addition to individual competitions, group performances are also very meaningful. Like this year's Games, various countries had large-scale performances with thousands of people, including various group exercises and dances, some expressing the martial spirit of the nation, and others promoting their inherent arts. Our country should also participate in group performances in the next Games. China's sports policy should be fundamentally reformed, starting from the family, to make parents aware of the importance of children's sports, cultivate their adventurousness, and focus on basic training. Chinese people eat too well, but lack nutrition, resulting in uneven physical development, which is also a major problem. The next Olympics will be in Italy, which is eight years away, but Italy has already started building the venue, on a scale larger than Germany's. That is truly planning ahead, and their dedication is admirable."

"What are your impressions of the emerging trends in various countries?"

"Our trip was aimed at studying sports in various countries, but we also paid attention to local customs and national conditions, and the education system. I personally found the most satisfying aspects to be the comfortable lives of the Danish people and the solemn courtesy towards foreign guests, which demonstrated the high level of the people. Denmark has stricter compulsory education than other countries, with almost all children aged six to fourteen receiving national education. The Swedish people are not much different from the Danish. Germany's material construction is the most magnificent and grand. The Italian nation is fiercely arrogant! Public sports in Czechoslovakia are the most widespread, with everyone receiving the benefits of physical education. When sports meets are held, hundreds of thousands of people participate in performances, which is incredibly exciting. In many emerging European countries, people's patriotic sentiments are very high. Among them, the Hungarians left the deepest impression on me. When we left Hungary, an employee of the hotel asked the delegation to sign their names. Mr. Hao Gengsheng wrote, 'May our beautiful rivers and mountains soon return to their rightful owners.' After explaining the meaning, the employee immediately shed tears, showing an unparalleled fervor for national restoration. At the main transportation hub in Budapest, there is a park that flies a half-mast flag all year round, reportedly to be raised to full mast after the country's territory is restored. The park is decorated with various national humiliation slogans made of flowers and plants, which are startling. Four stone statues stand at the corners, with rough textures and ugly faces, representing the four lost territories. Each time a territory is recovered, one statue will be smashed. Furthermore, the layers of postal postcards are printed with maps, showing the location of the lost territories at a glance. Just mentioning a few points can prove the depth of the Hungarian people's commemoration of national humiliation. Looking back at our country, we have lost more territory and suffered deeper national humiliation, but how does the national patriotic sentiment of our people compare to that of the Hungarians? Take Germany, a newly rising country, for example. Munich (transliteration), the third largest city in Germany, is the birthplace of the German revolution. There, a National Humiliation Memorial Hall has been built, with six wreaths placed on top and the Tomb of the Unknown Heroes built beside it, with eight paulownia coffins, also commemorating the lost territories and honoring national heroes. When Germans pass by this place, they must salute to show their respect."

"After touring Europe, what are your opinions on the women of various countries?"

"The women of the countries I saw all wore simple clothes, especially in Germany and Italy. Unless they were at social banquets, you could hardly see high heels or makeup. But they were physically strong and had the same spirit of service as men. In Germany, labor service is not divided by gender. From the age of eighteen, one must join the labor corps and serve for one year. For example, the reception centers and dormitories for this year's Games were entirely staffed by male and female students, and those from middle schools and universities worked very seriously. Their spirit of hard work and endurance far exceeds that of Chinese youth."

We talked for a long time that day. The above paragraphs contain relatively profound meanings and are worth reporting truthfully to readers.

The five female members of the delegation to Europe were all alumni of Ginling College. The first person on the left is President Wu Yifang. The third person is Ms. Du.

National humiliation souvenirs in a park in Budapest: (Top center) Half-mast flag style (Bottom center) Floral slogans (Four corners) Commemorative stone statues

Overseas Chinese Fifteen-Year-Old Tennis Flower - Miss He Aiying's Tennis Skills

— Yingdai

This time, the Chinese athletes participated in the World Games, and the results were that every item ended up with the loss of the game, causing everyone to gasp in cold air; but on the other hand, we got a piece of gratifying news, that is, the Chinese Miss He Aiying, who resides in England, has made amazing progress in her tennis performance. In addition to winning the British Wimbledon Junior Group Championship, on September 22, she also won the singles championship of the French Women's Junior Tennis Tournament.

Miss He is only fifteen years old this year, and her parents went to England to do business a long time ago; therefore, she was born in England. She has been very lively since she was a child. Her parents also liked to play tennis after work, so Ms. He has had the opportunity to play tennis since she was a child, and her tennis skills have improved year by year like her age. However, her amazing tennis skills have not been discovered in England until two years ago, when she joined the junior competition at the age of thirteen, and then this overseas Chinese tennis flower was discovered.

In the past two years, Miss He has indeed had many amazing performances in London, because although she is so petite, British female tennis players, all of the second and third class, have been defeated by her. When we think back, in April of this year, after she participated in the women's singles competition of the Melbourne Tennis Club Open Tennis Tournament in London, every British female player was defeated by her until she entered the final week before being defeated by the British female tennis player Miss Dorothy Round. Originally, Miss Round was a first-class British female tennis player, and Miss He's body was petite, and her physical strength was far inferior to that of Miss Round, so her failure was expected, but during the competition, she had given Miss Round a great threat.

In September of this year, she participated in the Wimbledon Women's Singles in England and won the championship, taking away a large silver cup; but then on September 22, she defeated the famous Parisian female tennis player Glenier by 7-5, 5-7, 6-3 and won the French Junior Tennis Championship, the news spread and shocked the entire European sports community. Her tennis skills, in this way, have indeed been noticed by European tennis experts. Anyone who has witnessed her performance believes that her future is very bright.

Looking at the situation mentioned above, Miss He's tennis skills are probably impossible to find a second person in the country, right? She has won a lot of face for the Chinese people internationally. Such a female tennis player will easily become a first-class female player in a few years. I hope that the officials in charge of Chinese sports will not neglect this female tennis flower drifting in a foreign country. If she can represent China in international tennis competitions in the future, she will definitely be able to win honor for China because she is only fifteen years old now, and in the next few years, the progress of her tennis skills will be amazingly rapid, which can be expected. Undoubtedly, her future is the most promising.

Pregnancy and Nutrition

— Zifu

Pregnancy means that from that moment on, the mother's body is not only nourishing itself, but also nourishing a new life with vigorous vitality. Therefore, special attention must be paid to nutrition during this period. Even with good nutrition, pregnant women often do not exhibit a perfectly adequate nutritional state.

Many people experience dental problems during pregnancy. This is because the calcium needed to build the fetus's bones is taken from the teeth. Calcium not only nourishes the teeth, but also provides resistance to caries. Since the mother's calcium is taken by the fetus, the mother's resistance is reduced. During the summer pregnancy, it is easy to contract diseases such as tuberculosis if one is not careful. When a pregnant woman's body has a slight fever, it is sometimes a symptom of the early stages of tuberculosis, so a doctor must be consulted immediately for diagnosis.

Especially during the transition from summer to autumn, most ordinary people exhibit weakened gastrointestinal resistance and decreased appetite. Pregnant women during this period have even weaker resistance and require particularly good nutrition. They should eat more nourishing and rich foods and pay attention to methods of preventing weakness in order to maintain the mother's health. If symptoms of malnutrition occur, a doctor should be consulted immediately to determine what nutrients are lacking in the body. Then, the doctor should instruct them on what to consume so as not to affect the health of the mother and fetus. However, this still cannot be regarded as anything more than a remedial measure. In fact, it is best to pay attention in advance and consume foods that are rich and balanced in nutrients so as not to become malnourished.

Generally speaking, the nutrients necessary to maintain health and prevent weakness can be obtained from everyday foods. However, we should also pay attention to selecting foods that are of good nutritional value in our daily diet. At the same time, we should not be picky eaters, and all kinds of nutrients should be taken in appropriate amounts.

Another point to note is that one must have a strong digestive and absorptive gastrointestinal tract. To strengthen the function of the gastrointestinal tract, it is best to regularly consume things that can strengthen the tissue cells of the gastrointestinal tract and invigorate the digestive and absorptive functions. If one can do so and at the same time not be a picky eater of one or two items, then the necessary nutrients can be obtained from everyday foods.

The Subconscious (Part Two)

— Yin

Indeed, the carving company run by Liu Yifan had no business at all, relying entirely on his father to support him; and at the same time, he really had no intention of pursuing women. However, the lack of business was one thing, and not wanting to marry was another, and there was no such close relationship between the two as his friends and relatives thought, because Yifan, although he had no money, his father had expressed his willingness to help him get married several times, but he had refused. The real reason was that he still wanted to work hard to study his carving, hoping to achieve more success in art, and because his consciousness was so pure and constantly striving upward, he saw only a thin ray of light, and nothing else.

But after another half year or so, the subconscious action was performed by this young artist.

In the spring of this year, Liu ××, the commander of the Northwest Border Defense, was unfortunately injured and killed in the campaign to suppress the Red bandits. The central government and the local people had a good impression of General Liu, so they decided to build a bronze statue for him in Lanzhou. After several selections and biddings, the business unexpectedly fell into Liu Yifan's hands. He was naturally very excited, and after half a year, he had prepared all the models and stone bases. In order to save trouble during transportation, he decided to send one person to send all the necessary materials over first, and then set off himself, planning to move the remaining part of the work to Lanzhou. Once the idea was settled, he was happy that he had no family and did not need to be delayed, so on a autumn morning, he embarked on his journey.

First to Xi'an, then change to the long-distance bus on the Xi'an-Lanzhou Highway. Because the highway was too bad, this kind of car often ran sometimes and sometimes not. The day Yifan arrived in Xi'an, it was unfortunate that there were some problems on the highway again, and the highway bureau temporarily announced the suspension of traffic. Yifan had to stay temporarily at the Xi'an Guest House of the China Travel Service. He had nothing to do at night and went to bed very early. Unexpectedly, he was suddenly awakened by a rude noise in the middle of the night. He listened carefully and it seemed that someone was fighting next door, and there was also a woman crying. At first, he thought that some bandits had come and was very panicked. Later, after listening carefully, there seemed to be people inside persuading him, and the woman's crying was not very urgent, which was different from the usual situation of robbery. Yifan was relieved; but the man still stretched his rough, hoarse voice and scolded as much as possible, and the woman also cried as much as possible, which really made Yifan unable to sleep. After a long time, probably the accountant went in to persuade them, and the quarrel between the couple stopped, but the sky was almost dawn.

The next day, the bus actually ran. When Yifan hired a car from the guest house to the station, he saw a fat man in military uniform taking a woman behind him to call for a car; when he arrived at the station, it happened that the fat man was also buying tickets, and he was also buying tickets to Lanzhou. Yifan originally had no need to pay attention to them, so he pretended not to see them, but when he heard the fat man speak, the voice was very familiar. After thinking about it, it turned out that he was the one who had scolded his wife last night.

Special Piece

The Shanghai Women and Children's Education and Welfare Home Over the Past Fifteen Years (Part One)

— Liu Wang Liming

The Motivation for the Launch

The Chinese Women's Temperance Movement began fifty years ago in Zhenjiang. When this trend surged from the Yangtze River basin to both sides of the Huangpu River, women in Shanghai also had many temperance organizations, including the Shanghai South and North Women's Temperance Societies, as well as the Student Temperance Society and the Children's Temperance Army. At that time, the president was Dr. Shi Meiyu, and the staff members included Ms. Mei Yunying, Ms. Liu Jingfang, and myself. The launch of this Shanghai Women and Children's Education and Welfare Home is closely related to me. At first, I was responsible for the youth work in the association. One day, the Shanghai Temperance Student Federation held a discussion meeting in my office. I said that the association's youth members, in addition to personally abstaining from tobacco, alcohol, gambling, and evil, should unite to do something that is really beneficial to society. At that time, I had just returned from overseas and saw that the streets in other countries were neatly organized. I proposed to establish a women and children's education and welfare home in Shanghai to accommodate and educate some of the wandering women, children, and beggars on the streets, as well as other unfortunate people, and to pioneer the anti-beggary movement, giving a lifeline to those in desperate situations. The emotions of the young people were as hot as fire. After my advocacy, everyone raised their hands in agreement, and the Shanghai Women and Children's Education and Welfare Home was conceived at this time.

The Opening Fee of Four Hundred Yuan

The principle of establishing the Shanghai Women and Children's Education and Welfare Home was approved, and the second step of work was to draft the articles of association. The third and difficult step of work began. Everyone felt their pockets, and the most they had was only five yuan. To start an education and welfare home with this amount, at least half a year must be maintained. What an impossible thing this is! So when the chairman proposed to discuss the budget, everyone lowered their heads, and some may have regretted that they should not have been so excited at the beginning.

At this time, I stood up and said: "No matter what we do, as long as we have the determination, we can always do it. Like this work of saving beggars, there must be many sympathetic people in the city. How about we hold a charity show?"

The atmosphere of hope, joy, and courage returned to the meeting room. In less than ten minutes of discussion, everyone decided to hold a charity show, and I was elected to write a drama, and they were responsible for the rest of the programs.

In Shanghai, the places of entertainment are the best in the country. In the crowd who are infatuated with foreign movies and Chinese Peking opera, it is not easy to hold an ordinary charity show!

"Since you plan to do it, don't be afraid." I encouraged the members with this spirit. Finally, Mr. Zheng Zegu and Mr. Zheng Zhengdi of the Mingxing Film Company and a large group of actors were also invited to help. Later, I couldn't find anyone to play the main role, so I had to take on the role myself.

The Xin Wutai on Wumu Land was the location for the performance. A total of about 900 yuan of tickets were sold, but after paying 300 yuan for the stage fee and 200 yuan for printing, transportation, equipment, and other fees, the balance at the time of the final clearance was only 400 yuan, which was the founding fee of the Shanghai Women and Children's Education and Welfare Home!

From Ximen to Jiangwan

The ancients said that "starting a business is difficult", but "maintaining a business" and developing it is even more difficult. Within two or three years, the enthusiastic young members moved away, found jobs, went to school, got married, and so on. Except for myself, there were almost no second person left. Fortunately, at this time, the competent authority—the Chinese Women's Temperance Association—itself underwent a huge change in its organization, changing from a president system to a board of directors system. I took the opportunity to reorganize the association's work, establishing three departments: Drug Resistance, Family Harmony, and Beggar Relief, and placing the Shanghai Women and Children's Education and Welfare Home under the Beggar Relief Department. Although the name has now been changed to the Social Service Department due to the development of the business. Four hundred yuan is indeed a very small amount to start a charitable organization, but in order to implement their original intentions and the credibility of society, the colleagues and others were even more courageous and established this tool for rescuing beggars—the Hai Women and Children's Education and Welfare Home—in a poor people's residence in Ximen.

Thriving National Arts Competition: Wrestlers Abundant in Talent; Women's Archery Features Prominent Figures; Weightlifting Competition Includes Women Today

Yesterday, the National Arts group held wrestling preliminary rounds in the morning and wrestling semi-finals in the afternoon, as well as men's and women's archery and pellet shooting competitions. A total of twenty-four people participated in wrestling, including two women. However, due to significant differences in weight and different levels, the women were canceled from the competition. Eight men were divided into lightweight and middleweight classes, with Tong Zhongyi, Wang Ziping, Wu Jianquan, and Liu Desheng serving as judges. Yarn and Cotton

Yarn Prices Too High, Guest Merchants Take Profits and Sell;

Forward Sales Particularly Brisk;

Market Suddenly Reports a Decline

The yarn market, which had been rising sharply, suddenly reported a decline yesterday. However, a certain merchant has already turned from short to long. According to market rumors, there is talk of a coordinated short squeeze in the November contract, so the November contract is standing alone. This month, they are determined to take delivery. However, current yarn business is turning sluggish because prices are too high, customers are pausing, and some guest merchants are taking profits and selling. Therefore, November yarn currently has a priority position due to the lack of spot yarn. However, it is still early; if spot yarn is quiet, the factory's position should loosen, and as prices have reached a high level, transactions have greatly decreased. The market closed at 4:00 PM.

At the opening of the tagged yarn market, a certain gentleman's plan to take delivery this month caused a firm rise of 5 jiao. Other forward months also rose 2-3 jiao. Again, Again Another Week of Inside Story of the Sharp Rise and Fall of Cotton Yarn

The standard cotton yarn market has experienced a dramatic rise since Monday of this week, like a raging horse. The front three months of contracts all reached their daily limit, and market sentiment reached a peak. The market situation was extremely chaotic, and both long and short parties frequently entered and exited with chips. The daily auction closed late at night, a new record in the history of the exchange. This month's cotton yarn happens to be approaching the delivery period. General floating accounts, in view of the improved environment, are eager to cover, so the price skyrocketed 20 yuan in three days. The reason for the increase is said to be active yarn sales, empty spot goods, and a short squeeze. On the one hand, spot traders are particularly eager to hoard, and at the same time, a major player has turned from short to long. For a time, the chips were insufficient to circulate, and they raised each other, so the rise continued and reached a new peak in five years. This month's cotton had Chen coarse lint cotton delivered. Following this, the old and new long companies from before had disputes over mortgage issues. The cotton stacked in various warehouses could not be inspected under escrow, and it was feared that it would be difficult to fulfill the delivery, so people were panicked, and the rise became more intense. The October cotton contract jumped 2.1 yuan in one day on the 21st to 43.5 yuan, also jumping 3.55 yuan compared to the price on the 17th of this month. Then, on the 22nd, the market situation took a sharp turn for the worse, with the price plummeting 1.55 yuan in the first session. According to market rumors, the board of directors held a late-night meeting. As a result, if the long party takes delivery, they will first collect the warehouse receipts, and the authorities will be responsible for recovering compensation if unqualified, out-of-shape situations occur after inspection. A storm has temporarily subsided, so the long party is greatly disappointed, and the market price quickly fell back. Today, the market has gradually calmed down, and transactions between the two sides have greatly decreased. In fact, after days of frantic rises and sharp falls, both sides are exhausted. The exchange also added two special gold batches to curb new trading, so transactions have naturally decreased. Moreover, the market price has risen too much, and more and more customers have taken profits and sold. News reports that speculation will be curbed, so the market trend has become more moderate. Spot yarn and thread have fallen back sharply, and customer sales have entered a state of stagnation due to excessive prices. It is found that the spot yarn price has fallen back 7-9 yuan compared to the peak price on the 23rd, and the 42-count thread price has fallen sharply by 46 yuan. The tagged yarn has only fallen back 2.5 yuan, and the tagged cotton has also fallen back 2.5 yuan. This huge change is rare in history. However, there are rumors that a certain gentleman in the November contract is undergoing a short squeeze. The future depends on actual needs. Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund: Examination for the Fifth Group of Students to Study Abroad to be Held Next Spring

(Nanjing, 23rd) The second group of twenty-six government-funded students to study in the UK under the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Fund will obtain their degrees and return to the country to serve next summer. The quota for the fifth examination has been set at twenty-nine, and the candidates have been assigned their examination venues. It has been decided that the examination will be held next spring. All detailed regulations are currently being drafted and are expected to be announced by the end of the year.

Education News

This City's Boy Scout Community Responds to the "One Day's Contribution to the Nation" Movement: Order Issued Yesterday to All Members for Consistent Implementation

The Boy Scout Council of this city, considering the gravity of the national crisis and the urgency of the diplomatic situation, believes that all compatriots should contribute their financial resources to the nation and make final preparations to support diplomacy. Yesterday, they responded to the "One Day's Contribution to the Nation Movement" initiated by the Lipo newspaper and issued an order to all members for consistent implementation. The original order is as follows: "For your compliance, this Council finds that the 'One Day's Contribution to the Nation Movement' initiated by this city's Lipo newspaper is deeply meaningful, and this Council should also actively promote it. It has been decided that on the 31st of this month, all service personnel and Boy Scouts in this city will donate all income and savings from that day to the purchase of airplanes for celebrating birthdays. Please submit the corresponding funds to this Council by November 3rd for consolidation and remittance. This is of utmost importance. This order."

Shanghai Universities Host a Public Banquet for Professor Aves and He Delivers a Lecture at Jiaotong University and Daxia University

Shanghai universities held a public banquet for Professor Aves of the University of London, England, at the International YMCA yesterday at 7:00 PM. Li Zhaoshi delivered a speech and introduced Professor Aves' lecture on the current situation of British universities, stating that the British government completely adopts a laissez-faire policy towards university education, but the government provides substantial subsidies to each university every year, setting up committees to investigate the needs of each school and provide subsidies. Professor Aves believes that there are quite a few people in England who are interested in China, but there are still some people who are not familiar with China, so he hopes that Chinese universities will send more professors to England to promote Chinese culture. Professor Aves believes that Chinese culture will make a great contribution to the future world. Finally, the professors present engaged in mutual Q&A with Professor Aves.

Daxia University invited Professor Aves to give a lecture at 3:00 PM yesterday, and Deputy Principal Ou, Dean Lu, and many professors hosted him. Professor Aves spoke about modern England. Professor Aves also lectured at Jiaotong University the day before yesterday.

Recent Overview of Higher Education Nationwide

(Nanjing, 23rd) The Ministry of Education, based on the statistical results of the 23rd year, has compiled a recent overview of higher education nationwide. There are a total of 110 colleges and universities, with over 11,400 faculty and staff, over 41,700 students, over 9,600 graduates, annual income and expenditure of over 35 million yuan, and over 4.87 million books.

Chinese Football League Zhongzi Group: Fudan vs. Yousheng This Afternoon at Fudan

The Shanghai Chinese Football Association will hold a Zhongzi Group league match between Fudan and Yousheng at the Fudan University Stadium this afternoon at 3:00 PM. The Huazi Group league match between Taiping and Guangdong, originally scheduled for tomorrow, has been postponed due to referee Liu Chunshu's unavailability.

Amateur Billiards Association Meeting

The Shanghai Amateur Billiards Association has designated its headquarters at 88 Nanjing Road starting this term. All competitions will begin on the 15th of next month. Those who wish to participate must register with Honorary Secretary Mr. Bi Li Que before the end of this month. The association's annual general meeting is scheduled to be held at the new headquarters at 5:30 PM the day after tomorrow (next Monday), at which new officers will be elected and other important matters will be discussed.

News from the Nursing School of the National Shanghai Medical College's Affiliated Hospital

The Nursing School attached to the First Affiliated Hospital of the National Shanghai Medical College (i.e., the First Hospital of the Chinese Red Cross) on Haige Road in this city has been in operation for more than ten years. Thirteen classes have graduated, totaling one hundred and sixty-eight students, who are serving in major medical institutions throughout the country, scattered in various places. The circumstances of each classmate are quite isolated from one another. In order to understand the service situation of each classmate, the school has specially organized an alumni association to connect feelings. The inaugural meeting was held at the school at 4:00 PM on October 20th. About fifty or sixty people attended. The initiators were Yin Cuihe, Liao Lihua, Chen Xiuyun, Sang Meiyuan, Guo Wenhu, Geng Xiwei, Zhou Xiduo, Ye Xiying, Li Xiyu, Yang Muying, Zhang Peiying, Wang Yun, Zhu Jiyao, Fan Shiliang, etc., a total of sixteen people. Ms. Chen Xiuyun was elected as the chairperson, Ms. Liao Lihua as the vice-chairperson, Geng Xiwei, Guo Xiuying, and Zhou Xi as secretaries, Fan Shiliang as the documentarian, Guo Wenhu as the accountant, and Zhu Jicang, Jin Qiu, and Fang Zhaorong as the annual publication editors.
